ğŸ”§ Opcjonalnie: Skonfiguruj Åšrodowisko Deweloperskie

Konfiguracja Kompilacji TypeScript
powershell
Zainstaluj zaleÅ¼noÅ›ci Node.js
npm init -y

Zainstaluj TypeScript i narzÄ™dzia deweloperskie
npm install -D typescript @types/node

UtwÃ³rz tsconfig.json
@"
{
  \"compilerOptions\": {
    \"target\": \"ES2020\",
    \"module\": \"ES2020\",
    \"moduleResolution\": \"node\",
    \"strict\": true,
    \"esModuleInterop\": true,
    \"skipLibCheck\": true,
    \"forceConsistentCasingInFileNames\": true,
    \"declaration\": true,
    \"outDir\": \"./dist\",
    \"rootDir\": \"./integration\"
  },
  \"include\": [\"integration/**/*\"],
  \"exclude\": [\"node_modules\", \"dist\"]
}
"@ | Out-File -FilePath tsconfig.json -Encoding UTF8

Skompiluj TypeScript
npx tsc

Dodaj skompilowane pliki do git
git add dist/
git commit -m "ğŸ“¦ Dodaj skompilowane moduÅ‚y integracji TypeScript"
git push


GitHub Actions dla Automatycznego WdroÅ¼enia
UtwÃ³rz .github/workflows/deploy.yml:
yaml

  push:
    branches: [ main ]

      uses: actions/setup-node@v3

        node-version: '18'
name: Zainstaluj zaleÅ¼noÅ›ci
      run: |
        npm install
name: Zbuduj TypeScript
      run: |
        npx tsc
name: WdrÃ³Å¼ na GitHub Pages
      uses: peaceiris/actions-gh-pages@v3
      with:
        github_token: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
        publish_dir: ./

### PLIK: DEVELOPER_GUIDE.md ###
ğŸ› ï¸ Developer Guide - Hip-Hop Universe

Przewodnik dla deweloperÃ³w chcÄ…cych przyczyniÄ‡ siÄ™ do rozwoju Hip-Hop Universe lub stworzyÄ‡ podobnÄ… platformÄ™.

ğŸ—ï¸ Architektura Systemu

Stack Technologiczny

Frontend
Framework: Next.js 13.5.6 (App Router)
Language: TypeScript 5.2.2
Styling: Tailwind CSS 3.3.7
Animations: Framer Motion 10.16.4
Icons: Lucide React 0.279.0
UI Components: WÅ‚asny design system

Backend
Runtime: Node.js 18+
Framework: Express.js 4.18.2
Database: SQLite 3 (development), PostgreSQL (production)
ORM/Query Builder: BezpoÅ›rednie SQL queries
CORS: Enabled dla cross-origin requests

Blockchain
Smart Contracts: Solidity 0.8.19
Framework: Hardhat 2.17.1
Network: Polygon Mainnet/Mumbai Testnet
Standards: ERC-20 (tokens), ERC-721 (NFTs)

DevOps
Containerization: Docker + Docker Compose
Process Manager: PM2
Proxy: Nginx (production)
CI/CD: GitHub Actions (planned)

Struktura Projektu

Instalacja i Uruchomienie

1. Klonowanie repozytorium:
bash

cd hip-hop-universe


2. Instalacja zaleÅ¼noÅ›ci:
bash
Root dependencies
npm install

Frontend dependencies
cd apps/web && npm install && cd ../..

Backend dependencies
cd backend && npm install && cd ..

Smart contracts dependencies
cd contracts && npm install && cd ..


3. Konfiguracja zmiennych Å›rodowiskowych:

env

NEXT_PUBLIC_BLOCKCHAIN_NETWORK=polygon-mumbai
NEXT_PUBLIC_CONTRACT_ADDRESS=0x...

env

4. Inicjalizacja bazy danych:

6. Uruchomienie aplikacji:

Terminal 2 - Frontend:

Aplikacja bÄ™dzie dostÄ™pna pod:

Database Schema

Core Tables
sql
-- Users and Authentication
CREATE TABLE users (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    wallet_address TEXT UNIQUE,
    username TEXT UNIQUE,
    email TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Artist Profiles
CREATE TABLE artist_profiles (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    stage_name TEXT,
    bio TEXT,
    specialization TEXT,
    verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    social_links JSON
);

-- NFT Collections
CREATE TABLE nfts (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    creator_id INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    title TEXT NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    price DECIMAL(18,8),
    token_id TEXT,
    metadata_uri TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Artist Tokens
CREATE TABLE artist_tokens (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    artist_id INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    token_name TEXT,
    symbol TEXT,
    total_supply BIGINT,
    current_price DECIMAL(18,8),
    market_cap DECIMAL(18,8)
);


ğŸ”§ Development Workflow

Git Workflow

1. Feature Branch Strategy:
bash
Tworzenie nowej funkcji
git checkout -b feature/new-feature-name
git commit -m "feat: add new feature description"
git push origin feature/new-feature-name

Pull Request do main branch


2. Commit Convention:

feat: nowa funkcjonalnoÅ›Ä‡
fix: poprawka bÅ‚Ä™du
docs: aktualizacja dokumentacji
style: zmiany formatowania
refactor: refactoring kodu
test: dodanie testÃ³w
chore: zmiany buildowania/CI


Code Style

TypeScript/JavaScript
typescript
// UÅ¼ywaj TypeScript dla wszystkich nowych plikÃ³w
interface ArtistProfile {
  id: string;
  stageName: string;
  bio?: string;
  specialization: Specialization[];
  verified: boolean;
}

// Async/await zamiast Promises
async function fetchArtistProfile(id: string): Promise<ArtistProfile> {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(/api/profiles/${id});
    return await response.json();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error fetching profile:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}


React Components
tsx
// Functional components z hooks
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

interface Props {
  artistId: string;
  onUpdate?: (profile: ArtistProfile) => void;
}

export function ArtistCard({ artistId, onUpdate }: Props) {
  const [profile, setProfile] = useState<ArtistProfile | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchArtistProfile(artistId)
      .then(setProfile)
      .finally(() => setLoading(false));
  }, [artistId]);

  if (loading) return <Loading />;
  if (!profile) return <NotFound />;

  return (
    <div className="artist-card">
      {/* Component JSX */}
    </div>
  );
}


Testing Strategy

Frontend Tests
typescript
// apps/web/tests/components/ArtistCard.test.tsx
import { render, screen } from '@testing-library/react';
import { ArtistCard } from '@/components/ArtistCard';

describe('ArtistCard', () => {
  it('renders artist information correctly', () => {
    render(<ArtistCard artistId="123" />);
    expect(screen.getByText('Artist Name')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });
});


Backend Tests
javascript
// backend/tests/routes/artists.test.js
const request = require('supertest');
const app = require('../src/server');

describe('Artists API', () => {
  test('GET /api/artists returns list of artists', async () => {
    const response = await request(app)
      .get('/api/artists')
      .expect(200);
    
    expect(response.body).toHaveProperty('artists');
    expect(Array.isArray(response.body.artists)).toBe(true);
  });
});


ğŸ” Security Guidelines

Frontend Security
Environment Variables: Nigdy nie commituj kluczy API
Input Validation: Waliduj wszystkie user inputs
XSS Protection: UÅ¼ywaj dangerouslySetInnerHTML ostroÅ¼nie
Content Security Policy: Konfiguruj CSP headers

Backend Security
Input Sanitization: Waliduj i sanitizuj wszystkie inputs
SQL Injection Prevention: UÅ¼ywaj parameterized queries
Rate Limiting: Implementuj rate limiting dla API
CORS Configuration: Konfiguruj CORS odpowiednio

Smart Contract Security
Reentrancy Protection: UÅ¼ywaj ReentrancyGuard
Access Control: Implementuj proper role-based access
Testing: Comprehensive test coverage dla contracts
Audits: Regular security audits przed deployment

ğŸš€ Deployment

Production Environment

Frontend (Vercel/Netlify)
bash

cd apps/web
npm run build

Environment variables w platformie:

Backend (VPS/Cloud)
bash
PM2 deployment

pm2 startup
pm2 save

Nginx reverse proxy
/etc/nginx/sites-available/hip-hop-api
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name api.hip-hop-universe.com;
    
    location / {
        proxy_pass http://localhost:4000;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
    }
}


Database (PostgreSQL)
sql
-- Migracja z SQLite do PostgreSQL
-- UÅ¼yj pgloader lub manual export/import
-- Update connection strings w .env


Docker Production
yaml

services:
  frontend:
    build: ./apps/web
    ports:
"3000:3000"
    environment:
NODE_ENV=production

    build: ./backend
    ports:
"4000:4000"

    environment:

### PLIK: DEVELOPER_GUIDE (1).md ###
ğŸ› ï¸ Developer Guide - Hip-Hop Universe

Przewodnik dla deweloperÃ³w chcÄ…cych przyczyniÄ‡ siÄ™ do rozwoju Hip-Hop Universe lub stworzyÄ‡ podobnÄ… platformÄ™.

ğŸ—ï¸ Architektura Systemu

Stack Technologiczny

Frontend
Framework: Next.js 13.5.6 (App Router)
Language: TypeScript 5.2.2
Styling: Tailwind CSS 3.3.7
Animations: Framer Motion 10.16.4
Icons: Lucide React 0.279.0
UI Components: WÅ‚asny design system

Backend
Runtime: Node.js 18+
Framework: Express.js 4.18.2
Database: SQLite 3 (development), PostgreSQL (production)
ORM/Query Builder: BezpoÅ›rednie SQL queries
CORS: Enabled dla cross-origin requests

Blockchain
Smart Contracts: Solidity 0.8.19
Framework: Hardhat 2.17.1
Network: Polygon Mainnet/Mumbai Testnet
Standards: ERC-20 (tokens), ERC-721 (NFTs)

DevOps
Containerization: Docker + Docker Compose
Process Manager: PM2
Proxy: Nginx (production)
CI/CD: GitHub Actions (planned)

Struktura Projektu


hip-hop-universe/
â”œâ”€â”€ apps/web/                 # Next.js frontend application
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ src/app/             # App Router pages and layouts
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ src/components/      # Reusable React components
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ src/lib/            # Utility functions and configs
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ public/             # Static assets
â”œâ”€â”€ backend/                 # Express.js API server
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ src/routes/         # API endpoint definitions
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ src/db.js           # Database connection and queries
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ sql/init.sql        # Database schema initialization
â”œâ”€â”€ contracts/              # Smart contracts (Hardhat)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ contracts/          # Solidity contract files
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ scripts/            # Deployment scripts
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ hardhat.config.js   # Hardhat configuration
â”œâ”€â”€ data/                   # Static data and configurations
â”œâ”€â”€ docs/                   # Documentation files
â””â”€â”€ docker-compose.yml      # Multi-service orchestration


ğŸš€ Konfiguracja Åšrodowiska

Wymagania Systemowe
Node.js: 18.0.0 lub nowszy
npm: 9.0.0 lub nowszy
Git: Najnowsza wersja
Docker: 20.0+ (opcjonalne)

Instalacja i Uruchomienie

1. Klonowanie repozytorium:
bash
git clone https://github.com/your-org/hip-hop-universe.git
cd hip-hop-universe


2. Instalacja zaleÅ¼noÅ›ci:
bash
Root dependencies
npm install

Frontend dependencies
cd apps/web && npm install && cd ../..

Backend dependencies
cd backend && npm install && cd ..

Smart contracts dependencies
cd contracts && npm install && cd ..


3. Konfiguracja zmiennych Å›rodowiskowych:

.env.local (w apps/web/):
env
NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL=http://localhost:4000
NEXT_PUBLIC_BLOCKCHAIN_NETWORK=polygon-mumbai
NEXT_PUBLIC_CONTRACT_ADDRESS=0x...


.env (w backend/):
env
NODE_ENV=development
PORT=4000
DATABASE_URL=./data/hip-hop-universe.db
CORS_ORIGIN=http://localhost:3000
JWT_SECRET=your-jwt-secret-here
POLYGON_RPC_URL=https://polygon-mumbai.g.alchemy.com/v2/...
PRIVATE_KEY=your-deployment-private-key


4. Inicjalizacja bazy danych:
bash
cd backend
npm run db:init
npm run db:seed


5. Kompilacja smart contracts:
bash
cd contracts
npx hardhat compile
npx hardhat run scripts/deploy.js --network mumbai


6. Uruchomienie aplikacji:

Terminal 1 - Backend:
bash
cd backend
npm run dev


Terminal 2 - Frontend:
bash
cd apps/web
npm run dev


Aplikacja bÄ™dzie dostÄ™pna pod:
Frontend: http://localhost:3000
Backend API: http://localhost:4000

Docker Development

Alternatywnie moÅ¼esz uÅ¼yÄ‡ Docker:

bash
Build i uruchomienie wszystkich serwisÃ³w
docker-compose up --build

W tle
docker-compose up -d

Zatrzymanie
docker-compose down

Database Schema

Core Tables
sql
-- Users and Authentication
CREATE TABLE users (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    wallet_address TEXT UNIQUE,
    username TEXT UNIQUE,
    email TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Artist Profiles
CREATE TABLE artist_profiles (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    stage_name TEXT,
    bio TEXT,
    specialization TEXT,
    verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    social_links JSON
);

-- NFT Collections
CREATE TABLE nfts (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    creator_id INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    title TEXT NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    price DECIMAL(18,8),
    token_id TEXT,
    metadata_uri TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Artist Tokens
CREATE TABLE artist_tokens (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    artist_id INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    token_name TEXT,
    symbol TEXT,
    total_supply BIGINT,
    current_price DECIMAL(18,8),
    market_cap DECIMAL(18,8)
);


ğŸ”§ Development Workflow

Git Workflow

1. Feature Branch Strategy:
bash
Tworzenie nowej funkcji
git checkout -b feature/new-feature-name
git commit -m "feat: add new feature description"
git push origin feature/new-feature-name

Pull Request do main branch


2. Commit Convention:

feat: nowa funkcjonalnoÅ›Ä‡
fix: poprawka bÅ‚Ä™du
docs: aktualizacja dokumentacji
style: zmiany formatowania
refactor: refactoring kodu
test: dodanie testÃ³w
chore: zmiany buildowania/CI


Code Style

TypeScript/JavaScript
typescript
// UÅ¼ywaj TypeScript dla wszystkich nowych plikÃ³w
interface ArtistProfile {
  id: string;
  stageName: string;
  bio?: string;
  specialization: Specialization[];
  verified: boolean;
}

// Async/await zamiast Promises
async function fetchArtistProfile(id: string): Promise<ArtistProfile> {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(/api/profiles/${id});
    return await response.json();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error fetching profile:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}


React Components
tsx
// Functional components z hooks
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

interface Props {
  artistId: string;
  onUpdate?: (profile: ArtistProfile) => void;
}

export function ArtistCard({ artistId, onUpdate }: Props) {
  const [profile, setProfile] = useState<ArtistProfile | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchArtistProfile(artistId)
      .then(setProfile)
      .finally(() => setLoading(false));
  }, [artistId]);

  if (loading) return <Loading />;
  if (!profile) return <NotFound />;

  return (
    <div className="artist-card">
      {/* Component JSX */}
    </div>
  );
}


Testing Strategy

Frontend Tests
typescript
// apps/web/tests/components/ArtistCard.test.tsx
import { render, screen } from '@testing-library/react';
import { ArtistCard } from '@/components/ArtistCard';

describe('ArtistCard', () => {
  it('renders artist information correctly', () => {
    render(<ArtistCard artistId="123" />);
    expect(screen.getByText('Artist Name')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });
});


Backend Tests
javascript
// backend/tests/routes/artists.test.js
const request = require('supertest');
const app = require('../src/server');

describe('Artists API', () => {
  test('GET /api/artists returns list of artists', async () => {
    const response = await request(app)
      .get('/api/artists')
      .expect(200);
    
    expect(response.body).toHaveProperty('artists');
    expect(Array.isArray(response.body.artists)).toBe(true);
  });
});


ğŸ” Security Guidelines

Frontend Security
Environment Variables: Nigdy nie commituj kluczy API
Input Validation: Waliduj wszystkie user inputs
XSS Protection: UÅ¼ywaj dangerouslySetInnerHTML ostroÅ¼nie
Content Security Policy: Konfiguruj CSP headers

Backend Security
Input Sanitization: Waliduj i sanitizuj wszystkie inputs
SQL Injection Prevention: UÅ¼ywaj parameterized queries
Rate Limiting: Implementuj rate limiting dla API
CORS Configuration: Konfiguruj CORS odpowiednio

Smart Contract Security
Reentrancy Protection: UÅ¼ywaj ReentrancyGuard
Access Control: Implementuj proper role-based access
Testing: Comprehensive test coverage dla contracts
Audits: Regular security audits przed deployment

ğŸš€ Deployment

Production Environment

Frontend (Vercel/Netlify)
bash
Build aplikacji
cd apps/web
npm run build

Environment variables w platformie:
NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL=https://api.hip-hop-universe.com
NEXT_PUBLIC_BLOCKCHAIN_NETWORK=polygon


Backend (VPS/Cloud)
bash
PM2 deployment
pm2 start src/server.js --name hip-hop-api
pm2 startup
pm2 save

Nginx reverse proxy
/etc/nginx/sites-available/hip-hop-api
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name api.hip-hop-universe.com;
    
    location / {
        proxy_pass http://localhost:4000;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
    }
}


Database (PostgreSQL)
sql
-- Migracja z SQLite do PostgreSQL
-- UÅ¼yj pgloader lub manual export/import
-- Update connection strings w .env


Docker Production
yaml
docker-compose.prod.yml
version: '3.8'
services:
  frontend:
    build: ./apps/web
    ports:
"3000:3000"
    environment:
NODE_ENV=production
      
  backend:
    build: ./backend
    ports:
"4000:4000"
    environment:
NODE_ENV=production
DATABASE_URL=postgresql://...
      
  db:
    image: postgres:15
    environment:
POSTGRES_DB=hip_hop_universe
POSTGRES_PASSWORD=secure_password

Code Style

TypeScript/JavaScript
typescript
// UÅ¼ywaj TypeScript dla wszystkich nowych plikÃ³w
interface ArtistProfile {
  id: string;
  stageName: string;
  bio?: string;
  specialization: Specialization[];
  verified: boolean;
}

// Async/await zamiast Promises
async function fetchArtistProfile(id: string): Promise<ArtistProfile> {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(/api/profiles/${id});
    return await response.json();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error fetching profile:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}


React Components
tsx
// Functional components z hooks
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

interface Props {
  artistId: string;
  onUpdate?: (profile: ArtistProfile) => void;
}

export function ArtistCard({ artistId, onUpdate }: Props) {
  const [profile, setProfile] = useState<ArtistProfile | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchArtistProfile(artistId)
      .then(setProfile)
      .finally(() => setLoading(false));
  }, [artistId]);

  if (loading) return <Loading />;
  if (!profile) return <NotFound />;

  return (
    <div className="artist-card">
      {/* Component JSX */}
    </div>
  );
}


Testing Strategy

Frontend Tests
typescript
// apps/web/tests/components/ArtistCard.test.tsx
import { render, screen } from '@testing-library/react';
import { ArtistCard } from '@/components/ArtistCard';

  it('renders artist information correctly', () => {
    render(<ArtistCard artistId="123" />);
    expect(screen.getByText('Artist Name')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });
});


Backend Tests
javascript
// backend/tests/routes/artists.test.js
const request = require('supertest');
const app = require('../src/server');

describe('Artists API', () => {
  test('GET /api/artists returns list of artists', async () => {
    const response = await request(app)
      .get('/api/artists')
      .expect(200);
    
    expect(response.body).toHaveProperty('artists');
    expect(Array.isArray(response.body.artists)).toBe(true);
  });
});


ğŸ” Security Guidelines

Frontend Security
Environment Variables: Nigdy nie commituj kluczy API
Input Validation: Waliduj wszystkie user inputs
XSS Protection: UÅ¼ywaj dangerouslySetInnerHTML ostroÅ¼nie
Content Security Policy: Konfiguruj CSP headers

Backend Security
Input Sanitization: Waliduj i sanitizuj wszystkie inputs
SQL Injection Prevention: UÅ¼ywaj parameterized queries
Rate Limiting: Implementuj rate limiting dla API
CORS Configuration: Konfiguruj CORS odpowiednio

Smart Contract Security
Reentrancy Protection: UÅ¼ywaj ReentrancyGuard
Access Control: Implementuj proper role-based access
Testing: Comprehensive test coverage dla contracts
Audits: Regular security audits przed deployment

  };

  // Tokenizuj collaborative asset
  const token = await modulFinansowy.tokenizujAktywoHipHop(
    wspolnyUtwor,
    artysta1 // gÅ‚Ã³wny twÃ³rca
  );

  // WypÅ‚aÄ‡ nagrody proporcjonalnie
  const Å‚Ä…cznaWspolpraca = 300; // 300 DRT
  
  await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(

    artysta2,

Scenariusz 3: Battle Hip-Hopowe

typescript
async function battleHipHop() {
  const uczestnicyBattle = [
    'mc_fire_001',
    'mc_ice_002', 
    'mc_earth_003',
    'mc_wind_004'
  ];

  const wynikiBattle = {
    zwyciezca: 'mc_fire_001',
    drugieMiejsce: 'mc_ice_002',
    uczestnicy: uczestnicyBattle,
    typBattle: 'freestyle_cypher'
  };

  // Nagrody battle
  const nagrody = {
    zwyciezca: 200,
    drugie_miejsce: 100,
    uczestnik: 25
  };

  // WypÅ‚aÄ‡ nagrody
  await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(
    wynikiBattle.zwyciezca,
    nagrody.zwyciezca,
    wygrana_${wynikiBattle.typBattle}
  );

  await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(
    wynikiBattle.drugieMiejsce,
    nagrody.drugie_miejsce,
    drugie_miejsce_${wynikiBattle.typBattle}
  );

  // Nagrody uczestnictwa
  for (const uczestnik of uczestnicyBattle) {
    if (uczestnik !== wynikiBattle.zwyciezca && 
        uczestnik !== wynikiBattle.drugieMiejsce) {
      await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(
        uczestnik,
        nagrody.uczestnik,
        uczestnictwo_${wynikiBattle.typBattle}
      );
    }
  }

  console.log(ğŸ¥‡ Battle ${wynikiBattle.typBattle} nagrodzony!);
}

ğŸ› ï¸ TROUBLESHOOTING

// SprawdÅº czy Gateway dziaÅ‚a

2. BÅ‚Ä™dy w tokenizacji

Problem: âŒ Tokenizacja nie powiodÅ‚a siÄ™

RozwiÄ…zanie:
typescript

ğŸ“š API REFERENCE

GÅ‚Ã³wne Metody

konwertujDRTnaEnergie(kwota, kontekst?)
Opis: Konwertuje tokeny DRT na punkty energii Å›wiadomoÅ›ci
Parametry: 
kwota: number - IloÅ›Ä‡ DRT do konwersji
kontekst?: string - Kontekst kulturowy (opcjonalny)
Zwraca: Promise<WzmocnienieEnergii>

sledzSukceArtysty(artysta)
Opis: Åšledzi sukces artysty i sprawdza ewolucjÄ™
Parametry: artysta: Artysta
Zwraca: Promise<WyzwalaczEwolucji | null>

tokenizujAktywoHipHop(dane, tworca)
Opis: Tokenizuje aktywa hip-hopowe (utwory, albumy, etc.)
Parametry: 
dane: any - Dane aktywa do tokenizacji
tworca: string - ID twÃ³rcy
Zwraca: Promise<any>

zaplacArtyscie(id, kwota, powod)
Opis: WypÅ‚aca nagrody artystom
Parametry: 
id: string - ID artysty
kwota: number - Kwota nagrody
powod: string - PowÃ³d pÅ‚atnoÅ›ci
Zwraca: Promise<any>

stakingDlaFunkcjiArtysty(id, kwota, funkcje)
Opis: Stakuj tokeny dla funkcji premium
Parametry: 
id: string - ID artysty
kwota: number - Kwota do stakingu
funkcje: string[] - Lista funkcji premium
Zwraca: Promise<any>

Metody Analityczne

pobierzStatusFinansowy()
Opis: Pobiera kompletny status finansowy moduÅ‚u
Zwraca: Promise<any> - Obiekt ze statusem

pobierzSaldoDrift(userId)
Opis: Pobiera saldo DRIFT uÅ¼ytkownika
Parametry: userId: string
Zwraca: Promise<any> - Saldo i aktywa

async function wspolpracaArtystow() {

  const artysta2 = 'dj_glebokiemysli_002';

  // UtwÃ³rz collaborative track
  const wspolnyUtwor = {
    typ: 'collaboration_track',
    tytuÅ‚: 'ÅšwiadomoÅ›Ä‡ w Duecie',
    wspÃ³Å‚pracownicy: [artysta1, artysta2],
    podziaÅ‚_zyskÃ³w: [0.6, 0.4] // 60-40 split
  };

  // Tokenizuj collaborative asset
  const token = await modulFinansowy.tokenizujAktywoHipHop(
    wspolnyUtwor,
    artysta1 // gÅ‚Ã³wny twÃ³rca
  );

  // WypÅ‚aÄ‡ nagrody proporcjonalnie
  const Å‚Ä…cznaWspolpraca = 300; // 300 DRT
  
  await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(
    artysta1,
    Å‚Ä…cznaWspolpraca * 0.6, // 180 DRT
    'wspolpraca_collaboration'
  );

  await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(
    artysta2,
    Å‚Ä…cznaWspolpraca * 0.4, // 120 DRT
    'wspolpraca_collaboration'
  );

  console.log(ğŸ¤ WspÃ³Å‚praca nagrodzona: ${Å‚Ä…cznaWspolpraca} DRT);
}


Scenariusz 3: Battle Hip-Hopowe

typescript
async function battleHipHop() {
  const uczestnicyBattle = [
    'mc_fire_001',
    'mc_ice_002', 
    'mc_earth_003',
    'mc_wind_004'
  ];

  const wynikiBattle = {
    zwyciezca: 'mc_fire_001',
    drugieMiejsce: 'mc_ice_002',
    uczestnicy: uczestnicyBattle,
    typBattle: 'freestyle_cypher'
  };

  // Nagrody battle
  const nagrody = {
    zwyciezca: 200,
    drugie_miejsce: 100,
    uczestnik: 25
  };

  // WypÅ‚aÄ‡ nagrody
  await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(
    wynikiBattle.zwyciezca,
    nagrody.zwyciezca,
    wygrana_${wynikiBattle.typBattle}
  );

  await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(
    wynikiBattle.drugieMiejsce,
    nagrody.drugie_miejsce,
    drugie_miejsce_${wynikiBattle.typBattle}
  );

  // Nagrody uczestnictwa
  for (const uczestnik of uczestnicyBattle) {
    if (uczestnik !== wynikiBattle.zwyciezca && 
        uczestnik !== wynikiBattle.drugieMiejsce) {
      await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(
        uczestnik,
        nagrody.uczestnik,
        uczestnictwo_${wynikiBattle.typBattle}
      );
    }
  }

  console.log(ğŸ¥‡ Battle ${wynikiBattle.typBattle} nagrodzony!);
}

ğŸ“š API REFERENCE

GÅ‚Ã³wne Metody

konwertujDRTnaEnergie(kwota, kontekst?)
Opis: Konwertuje tokeny DRT na punkty energii Å›wiadomoÅ›ci
Parametry: 
kwota: number - IloÅ›Ä‡ DRT do konwersji
kontekst?: string - Kontekst kulturowy (opcjonalny)
Zwraca: Promise<WzmocnienieEnergii>

sledzSukceArtysty(artysta)
Opis: Åšledzi sukces artysty i sprawdza ewolucjÄ™
Parametry: artysta: Artysta
Zwraca: Promise<WyzwalaczEwolucji | null>

tokenizujAktywoHipHop(dane, tworca)
Opis: Tokenizuje aktywa hip-hopowe (utwory, albumy, etc.)
Parametry: 
dane: any - Dane aktywa do tokenizacji
tworca: string - ID twÃ³rcy
Zwraca: Promise<any>

zaplacArtyscie(id, kwota, powod)
Opis: WypÅ‚aca nagrody artystom
Parametry: 
id: string - ID artysty
kwota: number - Kwota nagrody
powod: string - PowÃ³d pÅ‚atnoÅ›ci
Zwraca: Promise<any>

stakingDlaFunkcjiArtysty(id, kwota, funkcje)
Opis: Stakuj tokeny dla funkcji premium
Parametry: 
id: string - ID artysty
kwota: number - Kwota do stakingu
funkcje: string[] - Lista funkcji premium
Zwraca: Promise<any>

Metody Analityczne

pobierzStatusFinansowy()
Opis: Pobiera kompletny status finansowy moduÅ‚u
Zwraca: Promise<any> - Obiekt ze statusem

pobierzSaldoDrift(userId)
Opis: Pobiera saldo DRIFT uÅ¼ytkownika
Parametry: userId: string
Zwraca: Promise<any> - Saldo i aktywa

  // UtwÃ³rz collaborative track
  const wspolnyUtwor = {

    wspÃ³Å‚pracownicy: [artysta1, artysta2],
    podziaÅ‚_zyskÃ³w: [0.6, 0.4] // 60-40 split
  };

  // Tokenizuj collaborative asset
  const token = await modulFinansowy.tokenizujAktywoHipHop(
    wspolnyUtwor,
    artysta1 // gÅ‚Ã³wny twÃ³rca
  );

  // WypÅ‚aÄ‡ nagrody proporcjonalnie
  const Å‚Ä…cznaWspolpraca = 300; // 300 DRT
  
  await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(
    artysta1,
    Å‚Ä…cznaWspolpraca * 0.6, // 180 DRT

    artysta2,

  console.log(ğŸ¤ WspÃ³Å‚praca nagrodzona: ${Å‚Ä…cznaWspolpraca} DRT);

Scenariusz 3: Battle Hip-Hopowe

typescript
async function battleHipHop() {
  const uczestnicyBattle = [
    'mc_fire_001',
    'mc_ice_002', 
    'mc_earth_003',
    'mc_wind_004'
  ];

  const wynikiBattle = {
    zwyciezca: 'mc_fire_001',
    drugieMiejsce: 'mc_ice_002',
    uczestnicy: uczestnicyBattle,
    typBattle: 'freestyle_cypher'
  };

  // Nagrody battle
  const nagrody = {
    zwyciezca: 200,
    drugie_miejsce: 100,
    uczestnik: 25
  };

  // WypÅ‚aÄ‡ nagrody
  await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(
    wynikiBattle.zwyciezca,
    nagrody.zwyciezca,
    wygrana_${wynikiBattle.typBattle}
  );

  await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(
    wynikiBattle.drugieMiejsce,
    nagrody.drugie_miejsce,
    drugie_miejsce_${wynikiBattle.typBattle}
  );

  // Nagrody uczestnictwa
  for (const uczestnik of uczestnicyBattle) {
    if (uczestnik !== wynikiBattle.zwyciezca && 
        uczestnik !== wynikiBattle.drugieMiejsce) {
      await modulFinansowy.zaplacArtyscie(
        uczestnik,
        nagrody.uczestnik,
        uczestnictwo_${wynikiBattle.typBattle}
      );
    }
  }

  console.log(ğŸ¥‡ Battle ${wynikiBattle.typBattle} nagrodzony!);
}

ğŸš€ Techniczny Stack Ekosystemu

Integration: ethers.js + web3modal

AI/ML:
Style Analysis: TensorFlow.js
Recommendation Engine: Python + scikit-learn
Content Moderation: AWS Rekognition
Trend Prediction: Custom ML models

ğŸ”§ Techniczne Detale

JSON Schema Fields
Core Identity: id, displayName, alias, roleTags
Bio & Manifest: shortBio, manifestShort
Contact: email, website, social links
Web3: wallets (ethereum/polygon), tokens (SELPH/DRT)
Projects: array with id, title, type, description, status
Stats: respectPoints, followers, activeProjects, tokensMinted
Consciousness: vector array, stage, metadataUri
AI Integration: agentId, capabilities array
Monetization: revenueSplit, drops configuration

Security Considerations âœ…
No Private Keys: Wallet addresses set to null until secure setup
IPFS Placeholders: Real metadata URIs only after proper IPFS pinning
Email Protection: Use contact forms instead of direct email exposure
Permissions: Public profile flags for privacy control

Performance Optimizations âœ…
API Caching: 1-hour cache headers for profile data
Image Fallbacks: Default avatar on load error
Lazy Loading: Component-level data fetching
Error Boundaries: Graceful error handling

---

ğŸ“Š Integration Points

HipHopAgent.ts Connection
typescript
// PrzykÅ‚ad uÅ¼ycia w HipHopAgent

const consciousnessVector = profile.consciousnessProfile.vector;

// AI processing z consciousness data
const recommendations = await processConsciousnessRecommendations(consciousnessVector);


Consciousness NFT Minting
typescript
// Smart contract integration
const metadataUri = profile.consciousnessProfile.metadataUri;
const tokenId = await consciousnessNFT.mintConsciousness(
  userAddress, 
  metadataUri, 
  keccak256(JSON.stringify(profile.consciousnessProfile.vector))
);


DRT Token Integration
typescript
// Platform token usage
const drtBalance = await drtToken.balanceOf(userAddress);
const canMintNFT = drtBalance >= profile.monetization.drops[0].expectedPriceDRT;

ğŸ”§ Techniczne Detale

JSON Schema Fields
Core Identity: id, displayName, alias, roleTags
Bio & Manifest: shortBio, manifestShort
Contact: email, website, social links
Web3: wallets (ethereum/polygon), tokens (SELPH/DRT)
Projects: array with id, title, type, description, status
Stats: respectPoints, followers, activeProjects, tokensMinted
Consciousness: vector array, stage, metadataUri
AI Integration: agentId, capabilities array
Monetization: revenueSplit, drops configuration

Security Considerations âœ…
No Private Keys: Wallet addresses set to null until secure setup
IPFS Placeholders: Real metadata URIs only after proper IPFS pinning
Email Protection: Use contact forms instead of direct email exposure
Permissions: Public profile flags for privacy control

Performance Optimizations âœ…
API Caching: 1-hour cache headers for profile data
Image Fallbacks: Default avatar on load error
Lazy Loading: Component-level data fetching
Error Boundaries: Graceful error handling

### PLIK: QUICK_START.md ###
ğŸ”§ Quick Start Guide
Hip-Hop Universe + Rocket Fuell Girls Integration

âš¡ 5-Minute Deployment

1. Pre-Deployment Validation
bash
Navigate to integration directory
cd integration

Validate deployment readiness
node deploy.js validate


2. Environment Setup
bash
Copy environment template
cp .env.example .env

Edit required variables
notepad .env

Minimum required variables:
JWT_SECRET=your-super-secret-jwt-key-here
POSTGRES_PASSWORD=your-secure-db-password
MINIO_ROOT_USER=admin
MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD=your-minio-password


3. Start Integration
bash
Start all services
node deploy.js start

Monitor logs
node deploy.js logs


4. Verify Deployment
ğŸŒ Frontend: http://localhost
ğŸ” Auth Service: http://localhost:5000/health
ğŸµ Hip-Hop API: http://localhost:4000/api/health
ğŸ“¸ Rocket API: http://localhost:3000/api/health
ğŸ“Š MinIO Console: http://localhost:9001

---

ğŸ›¡ï¸ Security Checklist (CRITICAL)

âš ï¸ BEFORE PRODUCTION:

1. Age Verification (18+ Content)
javascript
// Implement in rocket-modified/server.js
app.use('/fantasy', (req, res, next) => {
    if (!req.session.ageVerified) {
        return res.redirect('/age-verification');
    }
    next();
});


2. Content Moderation
bash
Install content moderation
npm install @tensorflow/tfjs-node image-filter

Add AI content scanning
See SECURITY_AUDIT.md for implementation


3. DMCA Compliance
javascript
// Add to routes/integrations.js
router.post('/dmca/takedown', handleDMCATakedown);
router.post('/dmca/counter', handleDMCACounter);


4. SSL/HTTPS
bash
Generate SSL certificates
openssl req -x509 -nodes -days 365 -newkey rsa:2048 \
  -keyout nginx/ssl/private.key \
  -out nginx/ssl/certificate.crt


---

ğŸš¨ Emergency Procedures

Service Down
bash
Check service status
node deploy.js status

Restart specific service
docker-compose restart auth-service

View specific logs
docker-compose logs rocket-service


Database Issues
bash
Backup database
docker exec postgres pg_dump -U postgres hip_hop_universe > backup.sql

Restore database
docker exec -i postgres psql -U postgres hip_hop_universe < backup.sql


Emergency Content Removal
javascript
// Use admin API
fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/admin/emergency-disable', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + adminToken },
    body: JSON.stringify({ 
        assetId: 'asset-id-to-disable',
        reason: 'DMCA takedown / illegal content'
    })
});


---

ğŸ“ Support & Contacts

Technical Issues
Database: Check docker-compose logs postgres
Auth: Check docker-compose logs auth-service
File Storage: Check docker-compose logs minio

Legal Issues
DMCA: Implement takedown@yourdomain.com
Age Verification: Implement support@yourdomain.com
Privacy: Implement privacy@yourdomain.com

Production Monitoring
bash
Set up monitoring alerts
CPU usage > 80%
Memory usage > 90%
Failed auth attempts > 100/hour
File upload errors > 50/hour

    if (!req.session.ageVerified) {
        return res.redirect('/age-verification');
    }
    next();
});


2. Content Moderation
bash
Install content moderation
npm install @tensorflow/tfjs-node image-filter

Add AI content scanning
See SECURITY_AUDIT.md for implementation


3. DMCA Compliance
javascript
// Add to routes/integrations.js
router.post('/dmca/takedown', handleDMCATakedown);
router.post('/dmca/counter', handleDMCACounter);


4. SSL/HTTPS
bash
Generate SSL certificates
openssl req -x509 -nodes -days 365 -newkey rsa:2048 \
  -keyout nginx/ssl/private.key \
  -out nginx/ssl/certificate.crt


---

ğŸš¨ Emergency Procedures

Service Down
bash
Check service status
node deploy.js status

Restart specific service
docker-compose restart auth-service

View specific logs
docker-compose logs rocket-service


Database Issues
bash
Backup database
docker exec postgres pg_dump -U postgres hip_hop_universe > backup.sql

Restore database
docker exec -i postgres psql -U postgres hip_hop_universe < backup.sql


Emergency Content Removal
javascript
// Use admin API
fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/admin/emergency-disable', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + adminToken },
    body: JSON.stringify({ 
        assetId: 'asset-id-to-disable',
        reason: 'DMCA takedown / illegal content'
    })
});

ğŸš€ Hip-Hop Universe + Rocket Fuell Girls Integration Guide

ğŸ¯ Overview

This integration combines two powerful platforms:
Hip-Hop Universe: Music, NFTs, governance, and Web3 ecosystem
Rocket Fuell Girls: Model photography platform with content moderation

ğŸ—ï¸ Architecture


â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

ğŸ› ï¸ Quick Start

1. Prerequisites
bash
Install Docker and Docker Compose
docker --version
docker-compose --version

Clone repositories
git clone https://github.com/sobieranskip95patryk/hip_hop_universe.git
git clone https://github.com/sobieranskip95patryk/rocket_fuell_girls.git


2. Launch Integration Environment
bash
cd hip_hop_universe/integration
docker-compose -f docker-compose.integration.yml up -d


3. Access Services

| Service | URL | Description |
|---------|-----|-------------|
| API Gateway | http://localhost:8080 | Unified entry point |
| Hip-Hop Backend | http://localhost:4000 | Music & NFT API |
| Rocket Backend | http://localhost:3000 | Photo upload API |
| Auth Service | http://localhost:3333 | JWT authentication |
| Frontend | http://localhost:3008 | Next.js interface |
| MinIO Console | http://localhost:9001 | File storage admin |
| Grafana | http://localhost:3001 | Monitoring dashboard |

ğŸ” Authentication Flow

1. User Registration
javascript
// Register user for both platforms
const response = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/auth/register', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({
        username: 'artist_model',
        email: 'user@example.com',
        password: 'securepass123',
        role: 'artist', // or 'model' or 'user'
        artistName: 'MC Future',
        modelName: 'Anna Star'
    })
});


2. Login & Token Usage
javascript
// Login
const loginResponse = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/auth/login', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({
        username: 'artist_model',
        password: 'securepass123'
    })
});

const { accessToken } = await loginResponse.json();

// Use token for authenticated requests
const apiResponse = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/profiles', {
    headers: { 'Authorization': Bearer ${accessToken} }
});


ğŸ“ File Upload Integration

Hip-Hop Universe â†’ Rocket Fuell Girls
javascript
// Upload photo from Hip-Hop interface using Rocket backend
const formData = new FormData();
formData.append('photos', file);
formData.append('name', 'Artist Name');
formData.append('caption', 'Hip-hop inspired photoshoot');

const uploadResponse = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/rocket/upload', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Authorization': Bearer ${accessToken} },
    body: formData
});


Webhook Flow
When a photo is approved in Rocket Fuell Girls:
1. Rocket sends webhook to Hip-Hop Universe
2. Hip-Hop creates NFT opportunity
3. User gets notification about potential NFT mint

ğŸ—„ï¸ Database Schema

Unified Users Table
sql
CREATE TABLE unified_users (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE,
    -- Hip-Hop specific fields
    artist_name VARCHAR(100),
    genre VARCHAR(50),
    verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    -- Rocket specific fields  
    model_name VARCHAR(100),
    height INTEGER,
    location VARCHAR(100),
    -- Shared fields
    role VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'user'
);


Media Assets (NFTs + Photos)
sql
CREATE TABLE media_assets (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INTEGER REFERENCES unified_users(id),
    category VARCHAR(50), -- 'beat', 'photo', 'nft', 'video'
    file_path VARCHAR(500), -- MinIO S3 path
    thumbnail_path VARCHAR(500),
    -- NFT specific
    nft_token_id INTEGER,
    price_eth DECIMAL(18,8),
    -- Photo specific
    model_height INTEGER,
    approved BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE
);


ğŸ”— API Integration Examples

Cross-Platform Marketplace
javascript
// Get combined marketplace (beats + photos)
const marketplace = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/integrations/marketplace');
const data = await marketplace.json();

console.log(data.items); // Combined Hip-Hop beats and Rocket photos


User Profile Sync
javascript
// Sync artist profile to model profile
await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/integrations/sync-artist', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 
        'Authorization': Bearer ${accessToken},
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
        artistId: 123,
        artistData: {
            name: 'MC Future',
            genre: 'trap',
            verified: true
        }
    })
});


Cross-Platform Search
javascript
// Search users across both platforms
const searchResults = await fetch(
    'http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/integrations/users/search?q=future&type=artist'
);


ğŸ›¡ï¸ Security Features

1. JWT Authentication
Shared JWT tokens across platforms
Redis session management
Token refresh mechanism

2. File Upload Security
EXIF metadata removal
File type validation
Size limits (8MB max)
MinIO virus scanning

3. Rate Limiting
API endpoints: 10 requests/second
Auth endpoints: 5 requests/second
Nginx-level protection

4. Content Moderation
Admin approval workflow
Age verification for adult content
DMCA compliance tools

ğŸ“Š Monitoring & Analytics

Health Checks
bash

curl http://localhost:8080/api/auth/health


Analytics Dashboard
Access Grafana at http://localhost:3001 (admin/admin123) for:
User activity across platforms
Upload statistics
API performance metrics
Revenue tracking

ğŸš€ Deployment

Development
bash
Start all services
docker-compose -f docker-compose.integration.yml up -d

View logs
docker-compose logs -f

Stop services
docker-compose down


Production
1. Set environment variables:
   bash
   export JWT_SECRET="production_secret_key"
   export POSTGRES_PASSWORD="secure_db_password"
   export MINIO_ACCESS_KEY="production_access_key"
   

2. Enable SSL termination
3. Configure domain names
4. Set up monitoring alerts

ğŸ”§ Configuration

Environment Variables
env
Auth Service

DB_NAME=hip_hop_universe
DB_USER=hhuuser
DB_PASS=hhupass123

MinIO Storage

MINIO_ACCESS_KEY=hhuadmin
MINIO_SECRET_KEY=hhupass123

Service URLs
HIP_HOP_API_URL=http://hip_hop_backend:4000
ROCKET_API_URL=http://rocket_backend:3000
AUTH_SERVICE_URL=http://auth_service:3333


ğŸ› Troubleshooting

Common Issues

1. Database connection failed
   bash
   docker-compose logs postgres
   # Check if PostgreSQL is ready
   

2. MinIO bucket not found
   bash
   docker-compose exec minio mc mb /data/rfg-photos
   

3. JWT token invalid
   bash
   # Check auth service logs
   docker-compose logs auth_service
   

4. File upload fails
   bash
   # Check MinIO permissions
   docker-compose exec minio mc policy set public /data/rfg-photos
   

ğŸ“š API Documentation

Hip-Hop Universe Endpoints
GET /api/hip-hop/profiles/trending - Trending artists
GET /api/hip-hop/marketplace/items - NFTs and beats
POST /api/hip-hop/governance/proposals - Create proposal

Rocket Fuell Girls Endpoints  
POST /api/rocket/upload - Upload photos
GET /api/rocket/photos - Approved photos
POST /api/rocket/admin/approve/:id - Approve photo

Integration Endpoints
GET /api/hip-hop/integrations/status - Integration health
GET /api/hip-hop/integrations/marketplace - Combined marketplace
POST /api/hip-hop/integrations/sync-artist - Sync profiles

ğŸ› ï¸ Quick Start

1. Prerequisites
bash
Install Docker and Docker Compose
docker --version
docker-compose --version

Clone repositories
git clone https://github.com/sobieranskip95patryk/hip_hop_universe.git
git clone https://github.com/sobieranskip95patryk/rocket_fuell_girls.git


2. Launch Integration Environment
bash
cd hip_hop_universe/integration
docker-compose -f docker-compose.integration.yml up -d


3. Access Services

| Service | URL | Description |
|---------|-----|-------------|
| API Gateway | http://localhost:8080 | Unified entry point |
| Hip-Hop Backend | http://localhost:4000 | Music & NFT API |
| Rocket Backend | http://localhost:3000 | Photo upload API |
| Auth Service | http://localhost:3333 | JWT authentication |
| Frontend | http://localhost:3008 | Next.js interface |
| MinIO Console | http://localhost:9001 | File storage admin |
| Grafana | http://localhost:3001 | Monitoring dashboard |

ğŸ” Authentication Flow

1. User Registration
javascript
// Register user for both platforms
const response = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/auth/register', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({
        username: 'artist_model',
        email: 'user@example.com',
        password: 'securepass123',
        role: 'artist', // or 'model' or 'user'
        artistName: 'MC Future',
        modelName: 'Anna Star'
    })
});


2. Login & Token Usage
javascript
// Login
const loginResponse = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/auth/login', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({
        username: 'artist_model',
        password: 'securepass123'
    })
});

const { accessToken } = await loginResponse.json();

// Use token for authenticated requests
const apiResponse = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/profiles', {
    headers: { 'Authorization': Bearer ${accessToken} }
});


ğŸ“ File Upload Integration

Hip-Hop Universe â†’ Rocket Fuell Girls
javascript
// Upload photo from Hip-Hop interface using Rocket backend
const formData = new FormData();
formData.append('photos', file);
formData.append('name', 'Artist Name');
formData.append('caption', 'Hip-hop inspired photoshoot');

const uploadResponse = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/rocket/upload', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Authorization': Bearer ${accessToken} },
    body: formData
});


Webhook Flow
When a photo is approved in Rocket Fuell Girls:
1. Rocket sends webhook to Hip-Hop Universe
2. Hip-Hop creates NFT opportunity
3. User gets notification about potential NFT mint

ğŸ—„ï¸ Database Schema

Unified Users Table
sql
CREATE TABLE unified_users (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE,
    -- Hip-Hop specific fields
    artist_name VARCHAR(100),
    genre VARCHAR(50),
    verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    -- Rocket specific fields  
    model_name VARCHAR(100),
    height INTEGER,
    location VARCHAR(100),
    -- Shared fields
    role VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'user'
);


Media Assets (NFTs + Photos)
sql
CREATE TABLE media_assets (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INTEGER REFERENCES unified_users(id),
    category VARCHAR(50), -- 'beat', 'photo', 'nft', 'video'
    file_path VARCHAR(500), -- MinIO S3 path
    thumbnail_path VARCHAR(500),
    -- NFT specific
    nft_token_id INTEGER,
    price_eth DECIMAL(18,8),
    -- Photo specific
    model_height INTEGER,
    approved BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE
);


ğŸ”— API Integration Examples

Cross-Platform Marketplace
javascript
// Get combined marketplace (beats + photos)
const marketplace = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/integrations/marketplace');
const data = await marketplace.json();

console.log(data.items); // Combined Hip-Hop beats and Rocket photos


User Profile Sync
javascript
// Sync artist profile to model profile
await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/integrations/sync-artist', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 
        'Authorization': Bearer ${accessToken},
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
        artistId: 123,
        artistData: {
            name: 'MC Future',
            genre: 'trap',
            verified: true
        }
    })
});


Cross-Platform Search
javascript
// Search users across both platforms
const searchResults = await fetch(
    'http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/integrations/users/search?q=future&type=artist'
);


ğŸ›¡ï¸ Security Features

1. JWT Authentication
Shared JWT tokens across platforms
Redis session management
Token refresh mechanism

2. File Upload Security
EXIF metadata removal
File type validation
Size limits (8MB max)
MinIO virus scanning

3. Rate Limiting
API endpoints: 10 requests/second
Auth endpoints: 5 requests/second
Nginx-level protection

4. Content Moderation
Admin approval workflow
Age verification for adult content
DMCA compliance tools

ğŸ“Š Monitoring & Analytics

Health Checks
bash
Overall system health
curl http://localhost:8080/api/health

Individual service health
curl http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/health
curl http://localhost:8080/api/rocket/health
curl http://localhost:8080/api/auth/health


Analytics Dashboard
Access Grafana at http://localhost:3001 (admin/admin123) for:
User activity across platforms
Upload statistics
API performance metrics
Revenue tracking

ğŸš€ Deployment

Development
bash
Start all services
docker-compose -f docker-compose.integration.yml up -d

View logs
docker-compose logs -f

Stop services
docker-compose down


Production
1. Set environment variables:
   bash
   export JWT_SECRET="production_secret_key"
   export POSTGRES_PASSWORD="secure_db_password"
   export MINIO_ACCESS_KEY="production_access_key"
   

2. Enable SSL termination
3. Configure domain names
4. Set up monitoring alerts

ğŸ”§ Configuration

Environment Variables
env
Auth Service
JWT_SECRET=super_secret_jwt_key_2024
DB_HOST=postgres
DB_NAME=hip_hop_universe
DB_USER=hhuuser
DB_PASS=hhupass123

MinIO Storage
MINIO_ENDPOINT=minio:9000
MINIO_ACCESS_KEY=hhuadmin
MINIO_SECRET_KEY=hhupass123

Service URLs
HIP_HOP_API_URL=http://hip_hop_backend:4000
ROCKET_API_URL=http://rocket_backend:3000
AUTH_SERVICE_URL=http://auth_service:3333


ğŸ› Troubleshooting

Common Issues

1. Database connection failed
   bash
   docker-compose logs postgres
   # Check if PostgreSQL is ready
   

2. MinIO bucket not found
   bash
   docker-compose exec minio mc mb /data/rfg-photos
   

3. JWT token invalid
   bash
   # Check auth service logs
   docker-compose logs auth_service
   

4. File upload fails
   bash
   # Check MinIO permissions
   docker-compose exec minio mc policy set public /data/rfg-photos
   

ğŸ“š API Documentation

Hip-Hop Universe Endpoints
GET /api/hip-hop/profiles/trending - Trending artists
GET /api/hip-hop/marketplace/items - NFTs and beats
POST /api/hip-hop/governance/proposals - Create proposal

Rocket Fuell Girls Endpoints  
POST /api/rocket/upload - Upload photos
GET /api/rocket/photos - Approved photos
POST /api/rocket/admin/approve/:id - Approve photo

Integration Endpoints
GET /api/hip-hop/integrations/status - Integration health
GET /api/hip-hop/integrations/marketplace - Combined marketplace
POST /api/hip-hop/integrations/sync-artist - Sync profiles

3. Test integration with docker-compose
4. Submit PR with integration tests

ğŸš€ Hip-Hop Universe + Rocket Fuell Girls Integration Guide

ğŸ¯ Overview

This integration combines two powerful platforms:
Hip-Hop Universe: Music, NFTs, governance, and Web3 ecosystem
Rocket Fuell Girls: Model photography platform with content moderation

ğŸ—ï¸ Architecture


â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

ğŸ› ï¸ Quick Start

1. Prerequisites
bash
Install Docker and Docker Compose
docker --version
docker-compose --version

Clone repositories
git clone https://github.com/sobieranskip95patryk/hip_hop_universe.git
git clone https://github.com/sobieranskip95patryk/rocket_fuell_girls.git


2. Launch Integration Environment
bash
cd hip_hop_universe/integration
docker-compose -f docker-compose.integration.yml up -d


3. Access Services

| Service | URL | Description |
|---------|-----|-------------|
| API Gateway | http://localhost:8080 | Unified entry point |
| Hip-Hop Backend | http://localhost:4000 | Music & NFT API |
| Rocket Backend | http://localhost:3000 | Photo upload API |
| Auth Service | http://localhost:3333 | JWT authentication |
| Frontend | http://localhost:3008 | Next.js interface |
| MinIO Console | http://localhost:9001 | File storage admin |
| Grafana | http://localhost:3001 | Monitoring dashboard |

ğŸ” Authentication Flow

1. User Registration
javascript
// Register user for both platforms
const response = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/auth/register', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({
        username: 'artist_model',
        email: 'user@example.com',
        password: 'securepass123',
        role: 'artist', // or 'model' or 'user'
        artistName: 'MC Future',
        modelName: 'Anna Star'
    })
});


2. Login & Token Usage
javascript
// Login
const loginResponse = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/auth/login', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({
        username: 'artist_model',
        password: 'securepass123'
    })
});

const { accessToken } = await loginResponse.json();

// Use token for authenticated requests
const apiResponse = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/profiles', {
    headers: { 'Authorization': Bearer ${accessToken} }
});


ğŸ“ File Upload Integration

Hip-Hop Universe â†’ Rocket Fuell Girls
javascript
// Upload photo from Hip-Hop interface using Rocket backend
const formData = new FormData();
formData.append('photos', file);
formData.append('name', 'Artist Name');
formData.append('caption', 'Hip-hop inspired photoshoot');

const uploadResponse = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/rocket/upload', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Authorization': Bearer ${accessToken} },
    body: formData
});


Webhook Flow
When a photo is approved in Rocket Fuell Girls:
1. Rocket sends webhook to Hip-Hop Universe
2. Hip-Hop creates NFT opportunity
3. User gets notification about potential NFT mint

ğŸ—„ï¸ Database Schema

Unified Users Table
sql
CREATE TABLE unified_users (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE,
    -- Hip-Hop specific fields
    artist_name VARCHAR(100),
    genre VARCHAR(50),
    verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    -- Rocket specific fields  
    model_name VARCHAR(100),
    height INTEGER,
    location VARCHAR(100),
    -- Shared fields
    role VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'user'
);


Media Assets (NFTs + Photos)
sql
CREATE TABLE media_assets (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INTEGER REFERENCES unified_users(id),
    category VARCHAR(50), -- 'beat', 'photo', 'nft', 'video'
    file_path VARCHAR(500), -- MinIO S3 path
    thumbnail_path VARCHAR(500),
    -- NFT specific
    nft_token_id INTEGER,
    price_eth DECIMAL(18,8),
    -- Photo specific
    model_height INTEGER,
    approved BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE
);


ğŸ”— API Integration Examples

Cross-Platform Marketplace
javascript
// Get combined marketplace (beats + photos)
const marketplace = await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/integrations/marketplace');
const data = await marketplace.json();

console.log(data.items); // Combined Hip-Hop beats and Rocket photos


User Profile Sync
javascript
// Sync artist profile to model profile
await fetch('http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/integrations/sync-artist', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 
        'Authorization': Bearer ${accessToken},
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
        artistId: 123,
        artistData: {
            name: 'MC Future',
            genre: 'trap',
            verified: true
        }
    })
});


Cross-Platform Search
javascript
// Search users across both platforms
const searchResults = await fetch(
    'http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/integrations/users/search?q=future&type=artist'
);


ğŸ›¡ï¸ Security Features

1. JWT Authentication
Shared JWT tokens across platforms
Redis session management
Token refresh mechanism

2. File Upload Security
EXIF metadata removal
File type validation
Size limits (8MB max)
MinIO virus scanning

3. Rate Limiting
API endpoints: 10 requests/second
Auth endpoints: 5 requests/second
Nginx-level protection

4. Content Moderation
Admin approval workflow
Age verification for adult content
DMCA compliance tools

ğŸ“Š Monitoring & Analytics

Health Checks
bash
Overall system health
curl http://localhost:8080/api/health

Individual service health
curl http://localhost:8080/api/hip-hop/health
curl http://localhost:8080/api/rocket/health
curl http://localhost:8080/api/auth/health


Analytics Dashboard
Access Grafana at http://localhost:3001 (admin/admin123) for:
User activity across platforms
Upload statistics
API performance metrics
Revenue tracking

ğŸš€ Deployment

Development
bash
Start all services
docker-compose -f docker-compose.integration.yml up -d

View logs
docker-compose logs -f

Stop services
docker-compose down


Production
1. Set environment variables:
   bash
   export JWT_SECRET="production_secret_key"
   export POSTGRES_PASSWORD="secure_db_password"
   export MINIO_ACCESS_KEY="production_access_key"
   

2. Enable SSL termination
3. Configure domain names
4. Set up monitoring alerts

ğŸ”§ Configuration

Environment Variables
env
Auth Service
JWT_SECRET=super_secret_jwt_key_2024
DB_HOST=postgres
DB_NAME=hip_hop_universe
DB_USER=hhuuser
DB_PASS=hhupass123

MinIO Storage
MINIO_ENDPOINT=minio:9000
MINIO_ACCESS_KEY=hhuadmin
MINIO_SECRET_KEY=hhupass123

Service URLs
HIP_HOP_API_URL=http://hip_hop_backend:4000
ROCKET_API_URL=http://rocket_backend:3000
AUTH_SERVICE_URL=http://auth_service:3333


ğŸ› Troubleshooting

Common Issues

1. Database connection failed
   bash
   docker-compose logs postgres
   # Check if PostgreSQL is ready
   

2. MinIO bucket not found
   bash
   docker-compose exec minio mc mb /data/rfg-photos
   

3. JWT token invalid
   bash
   # Check auth service logs
   docker-compose logs auth_service
   

4. File upload fails
   bash
   # Check MinIO permissions
   docker-compose exec minio mc policy set public /data/rfg-photos
   

ğŸ“š API Documentation

Hip-Hop Universe Endpoints
GET /api/hip-hop/profiles/trending - Trending artists
GET /api/hip-hop/marketplace/items - NFTs and beats
POST /api/hip-hop/governance/proposals - Create proposal

Rocket Fuell Girls Endpoints  
POST /api/rocket/upload - Upload photos
GET /api/rocket/photos - Approved photos
POST /api/rocket/admin/approve/:id - Approve photo

Integration Endpoints
GET /api/hip-hop/integrations/status - Integration health
GET /api/hip-hop/integrations/marketplace - Combined marketplace
POST /api/hip-hop/integrations/sync-artist - Sync profiles

ğŸ”§ Konfiguracja

1. Podstawowa konfiguracja
typescript
import KonfiguracjaEkosystemu from './konfiguracja_ekosystemu';

const ekosystem = new KonfiguracjaEkosystemu("MojHipHopEkosystem");
await ekosystem.uruchomEkosystem();


2. Konfiguracja artysty
typescript
const artysta = await ekosystem.skonfigurujArtysty({
  id: 'polski_rapper_001',
  nazwa: 'MC KrakÃ³w',
  email: 'mc@krakow.pl',
  specjalizacja: 'rapper'
});


3. Tokenizacja utworu
typescript
const modulFinansowy = ekosystem.pobierzModulFinansowy();

const token = await modulFinansowy.tokenizujAktywoHipHop({
  nazwa: 'Warszawska Nokturna',
  artysta: 'MC KrakÃ³w',
  gatunek: 'Polish Rap',
  dlugosc: 240,
  opis: 'Autorski kawaÅ‚ek o stolicy',
  tagi: ['warszawa', 'rap', 'original']
}, artysta.id);


ğŸ“š API Reference

KonfiguracjaEkosystemu

uruchomEkosystem(): Promise<StatusUruchomienia>
Uruchamia caÅ‚y polski ekosystem Hip-Hop Universe.

Zwraca:
typescript
{
  status: 'sukces' | 'bÅ‚Ä…d';
  komunikat: string;
  aktywneModuly: string[];
  polaczeneDriftMoney: boolean;
}


skonfigurujArtysty(dane): Promise<Artysta>
Tworzy i konfiguruje profil artysty w systemie.

Parametry:
id: string - Unikalny identyfikator
nazwa: string - Nazwa artystyczna
email: string - Adres email
specjalizacja: 'rapper' | 'producer' | 'dj' | 'beatmaker'

generujRaportEkosystemu(): Promise<RaportEkosystemu>
Generuje szczegÃ³Å‚owy raport stanu caÅ‚ego ekosystemu.

ModulFinansowy

tokenizujAktywoHipHop(daneUtworu, artistaId): Promise<TokenizacjaRezultat>
Konwertuje utwÃ³r muzyczny na token cyfrowy.

zaplacArtyscie(artistaId, kwota, rodzajPlatnosci): Promise<TransakcjaDrift>
Dokonuje pÅ‚atnoÅ›ci na rzecz artysty.

stakingDlaFunkcjiArtysty(artistaId, kwotaStaking, okresStaking): Promise<StakingRezultat>
Uruchamia staking DRT dla artysty.

generujMozliwosciFinansowe(stanRdzenia): Promise<MozliwoscFinansowa[]>
Generuje moÅ¼liwoÅ›ci zarabiania na podstawie stanu Å›wiadomoÅ›ci.

ğŸ­ PrzykÅ‚ady UÅ¼ycia

Demo Kompletnego Systemu
typescript

await ekosystem.uruchomDemoPolskie();


Tworzenie Battle'a
typescript
const artysta1 = await ekosystem.skonfigurujArtysty({...});
const artysta2 = await ekosystem.skonfigurujArtysty({...});

const rozliczenie = await modulFinansowy.rozliczBattle(
  artysta1.id,
  artysta2.id,
  'artysta1', // zwyciÄ™zca
  500 // pula nagrÃ³d w DRT
);


Handel ÅšwiadomoÅ›ciÄ…
typescript
// Wystawienie stanu Å›wiadomoÅ›ci na sprzedaÅ¼
const oferta = await modulFinansowy.wystawStanSwiadomosci(
  artistaId,
  {
    poziom_energii: 95,
    stan_emocjonalny: 'euforia',
    preferencje_gatunku: ['trap', 'drill']
  },
  250 // cena w DRT
);

// Kupno stanu Å›wiadomoÅ›ci
const transfer = await modulFinansowy.kupStanSwiadomosci(
  kupujacyId,
  oferta.id
);

Saldo Artysty
typescript

console.log(Saldo: ${saldo.dostepne} DRT);

ğŸ›¡ï¸ PrzeglÄ…d BezpieczeÅ„stwa

Hip-Hop Universe obsÅ‚uguje wraÅ¼liwe dane uÅ¼ytkownikÃ³w, kryptowaluty i wÅ‚asnoÅ›Ä‡ intelektualnÄ…. Nasze podejÅ›cie do bezpieczeÅ„stwa obejmuje:

ğŸ”’ Web3 & Blockchain Security

Smart Contract Security

Audited Contracts
Wszystkie nasze smart contracts przeszÅ‚y audyt bezpieczeÅ„stwa:

solidity
// PrzykÅ‚ad zabezpieczonego kontraktu NFT
pragma solidity ^0.8.19;

import "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC721/ERC721.sol";
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/security/ReentrancyGuard.sol";
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";

contract SecureHipHopNFT is ERC721, ReentrancyGuard, Ownable {
    using SafeMath for uint256;
    
    // Reentrancy protection
    modifier nonReentrant() {
        require(!_locked, "Reentrant call");
        _locked = true;
        _;
        _locked = false;
    }
    
    // Rate limiting per user
    mapping(address => uint256) private _lastMintTime;
    uint256 private constant MINT_COOLDOWN = 300; // 5 minutes
    
    function safeMint(address to, string memory uri) 
        public 
        nonReentrant 
        onlyOwner 
    {
        require(
            block.timestamp >= _lastMintTime[to] + MINT_COOLDOWN,
            "Mint cooldown active"
        );
        
        _lastMintTime[to] = block.timestamp;
        uint256 tokenId = _tokenIdCounter.current();
        _tokenIdCounter.increment();
        _safeMint(to, tokenId);
        _setTokenURI(tokenId, uri);
    }
}

Connection Security
typescript
// Bezpieczne poÅ‚Ä…czenie z portfelem
export async function connectWallet(): Promise<WalletConnection> {
  try {
    // SprawdÅº czy portfel jest dostÄ™pny
    if (!window.ethereum) {
      throw new Error('No Web3 wallet detected');
    }
    
    // Request connection z timeout
    const accounts = await Promise.race([
      window.ethereum.request({ 
        method: 'eth_requestAccounts' 
      }),
      new Promise((_, reject) => 
        setTimeout(() => reject(new Error('Connection timeout')), 10000)
      )
    ]);
    
    // SprawdÅº network
    const chainId = await window.ethereum.request({ 
      method: 'eth_chainId' 
    });
    
    if (chainId !== POLYGON_CHAIN_ID) {
      await switchToPolygon();
    }
    
    // Waliduj adres
    const address = accounts[0];
    if (!ethers.utils.isAddress(address)) {
      throw new Error('Invalid wallet address');
    }
    
    return {
      address: address.toLowerCase(),
      chainId,
      connected: true
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    logSecurityEvent('wallet_connection_failed', error);
    throw error;
  }
}


Transaction Security

Secure Transaction Flow
1. Frontend Validation: Basic input validation
2. Backend Verification: Server-side double-check
3. Smart Contract Validation: Final on-chain validation

Gas Optimization & Protection
typescript
// Secure transaction handling
export async function executeSecureTransaction(
  contractMethod: ContractMethod,
  params: any[],
  options: TransactionOptions = {}
): Promise<TransactionResult> {
  
  // Estimate gas with safety margin
  const estimatedGas = await contractMethod.estimateGas(...params);
  const gasLimit = estimatedGas.mul(120).div(100); // 20% buffer
  
  // Check gas price isn't excessive
  const gasPrice = await provider.getGasPrice();
  const maxGasPrice = ethers.utils.parseUnits('100', 'gwei');
  
  if (gasPrice.gt(maxGasPrice)) {
    throw new Error('Gas price too high, try again later');
  }
  
  // Execute with timeout
  const tx = await contractMethod(...params, {
    gasLimit,
    gasPrice,
    ...options
  });
  
  // Monitor transaction
  const receipt = await tx.wait(2); // Wait for 2 confirmations
  
  return {
    hash: tx.hash,
    receipt,
    confirmed: receipt.confirmations >= 2
  };
}
