XSS Protection
typescript
// Input sanitization
import DOMPurify from 'dompurify';

export function sanitizeUserInput(input: string): string {
  // Remove dangerous HTML
  const clean = DOMPurify.sanitize(input, {
    ALLOWED_TAGS: ['b', 'i', 'em', 'strong', 'br'],
    ALLOWED_ATTR: []
  });
  
  // Additional validation
  if (clean.length > 1000) {
    throw new Error('Input too long');
  }
  
  return clean;
}

// Safe rendering
export function SafeUserContent({ content }: { content: string }) {
  const sanitized = sanitizeUserInput(content);
  
  return (
    <div 
      dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: sanitized }}
      className="user-content"
    />
  );
}


Authentication Security
typescript
// JWT token handling
export class SecureAuth {
  private static readonly TOKEN_KEY = 'hip_hop_token';
  private static readonly REFRESH_KEY = 'hip_hop_refresh';
  
  static storeTokens(accessToken: string, refreshToken: string): void {
    // Use httpOnly cookies in production
    const secure = process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production';
    
    document.cookie = ${this.TOKEN_KEY}=${accessToken}; secure=${secure}; samesite=strict; max-age=900; // 15 min
    document.cookie = ${this.REFRESH_KEY}=${refreshToken}; secure=${secure}; samesite=strict; max-age=604800; // 7 days
  }
  
  static async refreshToken(): Promise<string> {
    const refreshToken = this.getRefreshToken();
    if (!refreshToken) {
      throw new Error('No refresh token available');
    }
    
    const response = await fetch('/api/auth/refresh', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ refreshToken })
    });
    
    if (!response.ok) {
      this.clearTokens();
      throw new Error('Token refresh failed');
    }
    
    const { accessToken, refreshToken: newRefreshToken } = await response.json();
    this.storeTokens(accessToken, newRefreshToken);
    
    return accessToken;
  }
}


Backend Security

API Security
javascript
// Rate limiting
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');

const createRateLimit = (windowMs, max, message) => rateLimit({
  windowMs,
  max,
  message: { error: message },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  handler: (req, res) => {
    logSecurityEvent('rate_limit_exceeded', {
      ip: req.ip,
      path: req.path,
      userAgent: req.get('User-Agent')
    });
    res.status(429).json({ error: message });
  }
});

// Different limits for different endpoints
app.use('/api/auth/', createRateLimit(15 * 60 * 1000, 5, 'Too many auth attempts'));
app.use('/api/mint/', createRateLimit(60 * 1000, 3, 'Too many mint requests'));
app.use('/api/', createRateLimit(15 * 60 * 1000, 100, 'Too many requests'));


Input Validation
javascript
const Joi = require('joi');
const validator = require('validator');

// Schema validation
const userProfileSchema = Joi.object({
  stageName: Joi.string().min(3).max(50).pattern(/^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+$/).required(),
  bio: Joi.string().max(1000).optional(),
  email: Joi.string().email().optional(),
  socialLinks: Joi.object({
    twitter: Joi.string().uri().optional(),
    instagram: Joi.string().uri().optional(),
    youtube: Joi.string().uri().optional()
  }).optional()
});

// Validation middleware
function validateInput(schema) {
  return (req, res, next) => {
    const { error, value } = schema.validate(req.body);
    
    if (error) {
      logSecurityEvent('validation_failed', {
        error: error.details[0].message,
        path: req.path,
        ip: req.ip
      });
      
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: 'Invalid input',
        details: error.details[0].message
      });
    }
    
    // Sanitize
    req.body = sanitizeObject(value);
    next();
  };
}

function sanitizeObject(obj) {
  const sanitized = {};
  
  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {
    if (typeof value === 'string') {
      sanitized[key] = validator.escape(value.trim());
    } else if (typeof value === 'object' && value !== null) {
      sanitized[key] = sanitizeObject(value);
    } else {
      sanitized[key] = value;
    }
  }
  
  return sanitized;
}


SQL Injection Prevention
javascript
// Parameterized queries only
const db = require('sqlite3').verbose();

class SecureDatabase {
  static async getUserByWallet(walletAddress) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      // NEVER use string concatenation
      const sql = `
        SELECT id, username, email, created_at 
        FROM users 
        WHERE wallet_address = ? AND active = 1
      `;
      
      db.get(sql, [walletAddress.toLowerCase()], (err, row) => {
        if (err) {
          logSecurityEvent('database_error', err);
          reject(err);
        } else {
          resolve(row);
        }
      });
    });
  }
  
  static async createUser(userData) {
    const { walletAddress, username, email } = userData;
    
    // Validate inputs
    if (!ethers.utils.isAddress(walletAddress)) {
      throw new Error('Invalid wallet address');
    }
    
    if (!validator.isAlphanumeric(username, 'en-US', { ignore: '_-' })) {
      throw new Error('Invalid username format');
    }
    
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const sql = `
        INSERT INTO users (wallet_address, username, email, created_at)
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
      `;
      
      db.run(sql, [
        walletAddress.toLowerCase(),
        username,
        email || null
      ], function(err) {
        if (err) {
          if (err.code === 'SQLITE_CONSTRAINT_UNIQUE') {
            reject(new Error('User already exists'));
          } else {
            logSecurityEvent('database_error', err);
            reject(err);
          }
        } else {
          resolve({ id: this.lastID });
        }
      });
    });
  }
}


ğŸ“ Data Protection & Privacy

GDPR/RODO Compliance

Data Minimization
Zbieramy tylko niezbÄ™dne dane:
Wallet Address: Do identyfikacji uÅ¼ytkownika
Username: Do publicznej identyfikacji
Email: Opcjonalny, tylko dla notyfikacji
Profile Data: Tylko to co uÅ¼ytkownik Å›wiadomie udostÄ™pnia

User Rights Implementation
typescript
// GDPR user rights API
export class GDPRCompliance {
  // Right to Access (Art. 15)
  static async exportUserData(userId: string): Promise<UserDataExport> {
    const user = await db.getUserById(userId);
    const profile = await db.getArtistProfile(userId);
    const nfts = await db.getUserNFTs(userId);
    const transactions = await db.getUserTransactions(userId);
    
    return {
      personalData: {
        username: user.username,
        email: user.email,
        createdAt: user.created_at
      },
      profileData: profile,
      nftData: nfts.map(nft => ({
        title: nft.title,
        description: nft.description,
        createdAt: nft.created_at
      })),
      transactionData: transactions.map(tx => ({
        type: tx.type,
        amount: tx.amount,
        timestamp: tx.timestamp
      }))
    };
  }
  
  // Right to Erasure (Art. 17)
  static async deleteUserData(userId: string): Promise<void> {
    await db.transaction(async (trx) => {
      // Anonymize instead of delete for blockchain integrity
      await trx('users').where('id', userId).update({
        email: null,
        username: deleted_user_${userId},
        bio: null,
        deleted_at: new Date()
      });
      
      // Remove personal content
      await trx('artist_profiles').where('user_id', userId).update({
        bio: null,
        social_links: null
      });
      
      // Mark NFTs as from deleted user
      await trx('nfts').where('creator_id', userId).update({
        creator_id: null,
        creator_name: 'Deleted User'
      });
    });
  }
  
  // Right to Rectification (Art. 16)
  static async updateUserData(userId: string, updates: UserDataUpdate): Promise<void> {
    // Validate updates
    const schema = Joi.object({
      username: Joi.string().min(3).max(50).optional(),
      email: Joi.string().email().allow(null).optional(),
      bio: Joi.string().max(1000).allow(null).optional()
    });
    
    const { error, value } = schema.validate(updates);
    if (error) {
      throw new Error(Invalid update data: ${error.message});
    }
    
    await db.updateUser(userId, value);
  }
}


Data Encryption

At Rest Encryption
javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');

class DataEncryption {
  static encrypt(text, key) {
    const iv = crypto.randomBytes(16);
    const cipher = crypto.createCipher('aes-256-gcm', key, iv);
    
    let encrypted = cipher.update(text, 'utf8', 'hex');
    encrypted += cipher.final('hex');
    
    const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
    
    return {
      encrypted,
      iv: iv.toString('hex'),
      authTag: authTag.toString('hex')
    };
  }
  
  static decrypt(encryptedData, key) {
    const decipher = crypto.createDecipher('aes-256-gcm', key, 
      Buffer.from(encryptedData.iv, 'hex'));
    
    decipher.setAuthTag(Buffer.from(encryptedData.authTag, 'hex'));
    
    let decrypted = decipher.update(encryptedData.encrypted, 'hex', 'utf8');
    decrypted += decipher.final('utf8');
    
    return decrypted;
  }
}

// Encrypt sensitive data before storage
async function storeSensitiveData(userId, data) {
  const encryptionKey = process.env.DATA_ENCRYPTION_KEY;
  const encrypted = DataEncryption.encrypt(JSON.stringify(data), encryptionKey);
  
  await db.run(`
    INSERT INTO encrypted_data (user_id, encrypted_content, iv, auth_tag)
    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
  `, [userId, encrypted.encrypted, encrypted.iv, encrypted.authTag]);
}


ğŸ” Security Monitoring

Real-time Threat Detection

Anomaly Detection
typescript
class SecurityMonitor {
  private static suspiciousPatterns = [
    /script\s*:/i,
    /<iframe/i,
    /javascript:/i,
    /vbscript:/i,
    /onload=/i,
    /onerror=/i
  ];
  
  static detectXSSAttempt(input: string): boolean {
    return this.suspiciousPatterns.some(pattern => pattern.test(input));
  }
  
  static async logSecurityEvent(
    eventType: string, 
    details: any, 
    severity: 'low' | 'medium' | 'high' | 'critical' = 'medium'
  ): Promise<void> {
    const event = {
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      type: eventType,
      severity,
      details,
      ip: this.getClientIP(),
      userAgent: this.getUserAgent()
    };
    
    // Store in database
    await db.run(`
      INSERT INTO security_events (type, severity, details, ip, user_agent, timestamp)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
    `, [
      event.type,
      event.severity,
      JSON.stringify(event.details),
      event.ip,
      event.userAgent,
      event.timestamp
    ]);
    
    // Alert for critical events
    if (severity === 'critical') {
      await this.sendSecurityAlert(event);
    }
  }
  
  private static async sendSecurityAlert(event: SecurityEvent): Promise<void> {
    // Webhook do security team
    await fetch(process.env.SECURITY_WEBHOOK_URL, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        text: ğŸš¨ Security Alert: ${event.type},
        attachments: [{
          color: 'danger',
          fields: [
            { title: 'Severity', value: event.severity, short: true },
            { title: 'IP', value: event.ip, short: true },
            { title: 'Details', value: JSON.stringify(event.details, null, 2) }
          ]
        }]
      })
    });
  }
}


Smart Contract Monitoring
typescript
// Monitor smart contract events for suspicious activity
class ContractMonitor {
  static async startMonitoring() {
    const contract = new ethers.Contract(CONTRACT_ADDRESS, ABI, provider);
    
    // Monitor large transfers
    contract.on('Transfer', async (from, to, tokenId, event) => {
      // Check for suspicious patterns
      if (await this.isFlashLoanAttack(event)) {
        await SecurityMonitor.logSecurityEvent('potential_flash_loan_attack', {
          from, to, tokenId, txHash: event.transactionHash
        }, 'critical');
      }
      
      // Check for rapid successive transfers
      if (await this.isRapidTransfer(from, to)) {
        await SecurityMonitor.logSecurityEvent('rapid_transfer_detected', {
          from, to, tokenId
        }, 'medium');
      }
    });
    
    // Monitor failed transactions
    provider.on('pending', async (txHash) => {
      try {
        const tx = await provider.getTransaction(txHash);
        if (tx.to === CONTRACT_ADDRESS) {
          const receipt = await tx.wait();
          if (receipt.status === 0) {
            await SecurityMonitor.logSecurityEvent('contract_call_failed', {
              txHash, from: tx.from, gasUsed: receipt.gasUsed
            }, 'low');
          }
        }
      } catch (error) {
        // Handle monitoring errors
      }
    });
  }
  
  private static async isFlashLoanAttack(event): Promise<boolean> {
    // Detect rapid buy-sell patterns within same block
    const block = await provider.getBlock(event.blockNumber);
    const blockTransactions = await Promise.all(
      block.transactions.map(txHash => provider.getTransaction(txHash))
    );
    
    const contractTransactions = blockTransactions.filter(tx => tx.to === CONTRACT_ADDRESS);
    return contractTransactions.length > 10; // Suspicious if >10 contract calls in one block
  }
}


ğŸš¨ Incident Response

Security Incident Playbook

Severity Levels
1. Low: Pojedyncze prÃ³by atakÃ³w, automatycznie zablokowane
2. Medium: Wykryte wzorce atakÃ³w, wymagana analiza
3. High: Aktywny atak w toku, wymagana natychmiastowa akcja
4. Critical: Naruszenie bezpieczeÅ„stwa, potencjalna utrata Å›rodkÃ³w

Response Procedures

Critical Incident Response
typescript
class IncidentResponse {
  static async handleCriticalIncident(incident: SecurityIncident): Promise<void> {
    // 1. Immediate containment
    await this.enableEmergencyMode();
    
    // 2. Pause all critical operations
    await this.pauseSmartContracts();
    
    // 3. Notify security team
    await this.notifySecurityTeam(incident);
    
    // 4. Begin investigation
    await this.startInvestigation(incident);
    
    // 5. Communicate with users
    await this.notifyUsers('Service temporarily paused for security review');
  }
  
  private static async enableEmergencyMode(): Promise<void> {
    // Activate emergency circuit breaker
    await redis.set('emergency_mode', 'true', 'EX', 3600); // 1 hour
    
    // Block new transactions
    await redis.set('transactions_blocked', 'true', 'EX', 3600);
    
    // Enable enhanced monitoring
    await redis.set('enhanced_monitoring', 'true', 'EX', 3600);
  }
  
  private static async pauseSmartContracts(): Promise<void> {
    const emergencyWallet = new ethers.Wallet(
      process.env.EMERGENCY_PRIVATE_KEY, 
      provider
    );
    
    const contracts = [
      new ethers.Contract(NFT_CONTRACT_ADDRESS, NFT_ABI, emergencyWallet),
      new ethers.Contract(TOKEN_CONTRACT_ADDRESS, TOKEN_ABI, emergencyWallet),
      new ethers.Contract(MARKETPLACE_CONTRACT_ADDRESS, MARKETPLACE_ABI, emergencyWallet)
    ];
    
    for (const contract of contracts) {
      try {
        if (contract.pause) {
          await contract.pause();
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(Failed to pause contract ${contract.address}:, error);
      }
    }
  }
}


Recovery Procedures

Post-Incident Recovery
1. Vulnerability Assessment: PeÅ‚na analiza przyczyn
2. Patch Development: Szybkie poprawki bezpieczeÅ„stwa
3. Testing: Thorough testing w Å›rodowisku testowym
4. Gradual Restoration: Stopniowe przywracanie funkcji
5. Post-Mortem: Analiza incydentu i ulepszenia

ğŸ“‹ Security Checklist

Pre-Launch Security Audit

Smart Contracts
[ ] Wszystkie kontrakty audytowane przez zewnÄ™trznÄ… firmÄ™
[ ] Implementacja emergency pause mechanism
[ ] Reentrancy protection na wszystkich zewnÄ™trznych wywoÅ‚aniach
[ ] Access control dla wszystkich admin functions
[ ] Rate limiting dla user-facing functions
[ ] Input validation dla wszystkich parametrÃ³w
[ ] Event emission dla wszystkich krytycznych operacji

Backend API
[ ] Rate limiting na wszystkich endpoints
[ ] Input validation i sanitization
[ ] SQL injection protection (parameterized queries)
[ ] CORS properly configured
[ ] HTTPS enforced w produkcji
[ ] Authentication i authorization na wszystkich chronionych routes
[ ] Sensitive data encryption at rest
[ ] Proper error handling (nie wycieka internal details)

Frontend
[ ] Content Security Policy headers
[ ] XSS protection przez input sanitization
[ ] Secure authentication token handling
[ ] HTTPS-only cookies w produkcji
[ ] No sensitive data w localStorage
[ ] Proper logout implementation
[ ] Input validation przed wysÅ‚aniem do backend

Infrastructure
[ ] Database access restricted do aplikacji
[ ] Environment variables properly secured
[ ] Regular security updates dla wszystkich dependencies
[ ] Monitoring i alerting system
[ ] Backup i disaster recovery plan
[ ] Penetration testing completed

Ongoing Security Maintenance

Daily Tasks
[ ] Review security logs i alerts
[ ] Monitor transaction patterns dla anomalii
[ ] Check for dependency updates z security fixes
[ ] Verify backup systems dziaÅ‚ajÄ…

Weekly Tasks
[ ] Security metrics review
[ ] Incident response training
[ ] Update security documentation
[ ] Review user reports dla security issues

Monthly Tasks
[ ] Penetration testing
[ ] Security architecture review
[ ] Update incident response procedures
[ ] Team security training

Hip-Hop Universe obsÅ‚uguje wraÅ¼liwe dane uÅ¼ytkownikÃ³w, kryptowaluty i wÅ‚asnoÅ›Ä‡ intelektualnÄ…. Nasze podejÅ›cie do bezpieczeÅ„stwa obejmuje:

ğŸ”’ Web3 & Blockchain Security

Smart Contract Security

Audited Contracts
Wszystkie nasze smart contracts przeszÅ‚y audyt bezpieczeÅ„stwa:

solidity
// PrzykÅ‚ad zabezpieczonego kontraktu NFT
pragma solidity ^0.8.19;

import "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC721/ERC721.sol";
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/security/ReentrancyGuard.sol";
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";

contract SecureHipHopNFT is ERC721, ReentrancyGuard, Ownable {
    using SafeMath for uint256;
    
    // Reentrancy protection
    modifier nonReentrant() {
        require(!_locked, "Reentrant call");
        _locked = true;
        _;
        _locked = false;
    }
    
    // Rate limiting per user
    mapping(address => uint256) private _lastMintTime;
    uint256 private constant MINT_COOLDOWN = 300; // 5 minutes
    
    function safeMint(address to, string memory uri) 
        public 
        nonReentrant 
        onlyOwner 
    {
        require(
            block.timestamp >= _lastMintTime[to] + MINT_COOLDOWN,
            "Mint cooldown active"
        );
        
        _lastMintTime[to] = block.timestamp;
        uint256 tokenId = _tokenIdCounter.current();
        _tokenIdCounter.increment();
        _safeMint(to, tokenId);
        _setTokenURI(tokenId, uri);
    }
}


Key Security Features
Reentrancy Protection: Zapobiega atakom reentrancy
Access Control: Role-based permissions
Rate Limiting: Ochrona przed spam attacks
Input Validation: Walidacja wszystkich parametrÃ³w
Emergency Pause: MoÅ¼liwoÅ›Ä‡ zatrzymania kontraktu w razie problemÃ³w

Connection Security
typescript
// Bezpieczne poÅ‚Ä…czenie z portfelem
export async function connectWallet(): Promise<WalletConnection> {
  try {
    // SprawdÅº czy portfel jest dostÄ™pny
    if (!window.ethereum) {
      throw new Error('No Web3 wallet detected');
    }
    
    // Request connection z timeout
    const accounts = await Promise.race([
      window.ethereum.request({ 
        method: 'eth_requestAccounts' 
      }),
      new Promise((_, reject) => 
        setTimeout(() => reject(new Error('Connection timeout')), 10000)
      )
    ]);
    
    // SprawdÅº network
    const chainId = await window.ethereum.request({ 
      method: 'eth_chainId' 
    });
    
    if (chainId !== POLYGON_CHAIN_ID) {
      await switchToPolygon();
    }
    
    // Waliduj adres
    const address = accounts[0];
    if (!ethers.utils.isAddress(address)) {
      throw new Error('Invalid wallet address');
    }
    
    return {
      address: address.toLowerCase(),
      chainId,
      connected: true
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    logSecurityEvent('wallet_connection_failed', error);
    throw error;
  }
}


Transaction Security

Secure Transaction Flow
1. Frontend Validation: Basic input validation
2. Backend Verification: Server-side double-check
3. Smart Contract Validation: Final on-chain validation
4. Event Monitoring: Real-time fraud detection

Gas Optimization & Protection
typescript
// Secure transaction handling
export async function executeSecureTransaction(
  contractMethod: ContractMethod,
  params: any[],
  options: TransactionOptions = {}
): Promise<TransactionResult> {
  
  // Estimate gas with safety margin
  const estimatedGas = await contractMethod.estimateGas(...params);
  const gasLimit = estimatedGas.mul(120).div(100); // 20% buffer
  
  // Check gas price isn't excessive
  const gasPrice = await provider.getGasPrice();
  const maxGasPrice = ethers.utils.parseUnits('100', 'gwei');
  
  if (gasPrice.gt(maxGasPrice)) {
    throw new Error('Gas price too high, try again later');
  }
  
  // Execute with timeout
  const tx = await contractMethod(...params, {
    gasLimit,
    gasPrice,
    ...options
  });
  
  // Monitor transaction
  const receipt = await tx.wait(2); // Wait for 2 confirmations
  
  return {
    hash: tx.hash,
    receipt,
    confirmed: receipt.confirmations >= 2
  };
}

XSS Protection
typescript
// Input sanitization
import DOMPurify from 'dompurify';

export function sanitizeUserInput(input: string): string {
  // Remove dangerous HTML
  const clean = DOMPurify.sanitize(input, {
    ALLOWED_TAGS: ['b', 'i', 'em', 'strong', 'br'],
    ALLOWED_ATTR: []
  });
  
  // Additional validation
  if (clean.length > 1000) {
    throw new Error('Input too long');
  }
  
  return clean;
}

// Safe rendering
export function SafeUserContent({ content }: { content: string }) {
  const sanitized = sanitizeUserInput(content);
  
  return (
    <div 
      dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: sanitized }}
      className="user-content"
    />
  );
}


Authentication Security
typescript
// JWT token handling
export class SecureAuth {
  private static readonly TOKEN_KEY = 'hip_hop_token';
  private static readonly REFRESH_KEY = 'hip_hop_refresh';
  
  static storeTokens(accessToken: string, refreshToken: string): void {
    // Use httpOnly cookies in production
    const secure = process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production';
    
    document.cookie = ${this.TOKEN_KEY}=${accessToken}; secure=${secure}; samesite=strict; max-age=900; // 15 min
    document.cookie = ${this.REFRESH_KEY}=${refreshToken}; secure=${secure}; samesite=strict; max-age=604800; // 7 days
  }
  
  static async refreshToken(): Promise<string> {
    const refreshToken = this.getRefreshToken();
    if (!refreshToken) {
      throw new Error('No refresh token available');
    }
    
    const response = await fetch('/api/auth/refresh', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ refreshToken })
    });
    
    if (!response.ok) {
      this.clearTokens();
      throw new Error('Token refresh failed');
    }
    
    const { accessToken, refreshToken: newRefreshToken } = await response.json();
    this.storeTokens(accessToken, newRefreshToken);
    
    return accessToken;
  }
}


Backend Security

API Security
javascript
// Rate limiting
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');

const createRateLimit = (windowMs, max, message) => rateLimit({
  windowMs,
  max,
  message: { error: message },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  handler: (req, res) => {
    logSecurityEvent('rate_limit_exceeded', {
      ip: req.ip,
      path: req.path,
      userAgent: req.get('User-Agent')
    });
    res.status(429).json({ error: message });
  }
});

// Different limits for different endpoints
app.use('/api/auth/', createRateLimit(15 * 60 * 1000, 5, 'Too many auth attempts'));
app.use('/api/mint/', createRateLimit(60 * 1000, 3, 'Too many mint requests'));
app.use('/api/', createRateLimit(15 * 60 * 1000, 100, 'Too many requests'));


Input Validation
javascript
const Joi = require('joi');
const validator = require('validator');

// Schema validation
const userProfileSchema = Joi.object({
  stageName: Joi.string().min(3).max(50).pattern(/^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+$/).required(),
  bio: Joi.string().max(1000).optional(),
  email: Joi.string().email().optional(),
  socialLinks: Joi.object({
    twitter: Joi.string().uri().optional(),
    instagram: Joi.string().uri().optional(),
    youtube: Joi.string().uri().optional()
  }).optional()
});

// Validation middleware
function validateInput(schema) {
  return (req, res, next) => {
    const { error, value } = schema.validate(req.body);
    
    if (error) {
      logSecurityEvent('validation_failed', {
        error: error.details[0].message,
        path: req.path,
        ip: req.ip
      });
      
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: 'Invalid input',
        details: error.details[0].message
      });
    }
    
    // Sanitize
    req.body = sanitizeObject(value);
    next();
  };
}

function sanitizeObject(obj) {
  const sanitized = {};
  
  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {
    if (typeof value === 'string') {
      sanitized[key] = validator.escape(value.trim());
    } else if (typeof value === 'object' && value !== null) {
      sanitized[key] = sanitizeObject(value);
    } else {
      sanitized[key] = value;
    }
  }
  
  return sanitized;
}


SQL Injection Prevention
javascript
// Parameterized queries only
const db = require('sqlite3').verbose();

class SecureDatabase {
  static async getUserByWallet(walletAddress) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      // NEVER use string concatenation
      const sql = `
        SELECT id, username, email, created_at 
        FROM users 
        WHERE wallet_address = ? AND active = 1
      `;
      
      db.get(sql, [walletAddress.toLowerCase()], (err, row) => {
        if (err) {
          logSecurityEvent('database_error', err);
          reject(err);
        } else {
          resolve(row);
        }
      });
    });
  }
  
  static async createUser(userData) {
    const { walletAddress, username, email } = userData;
    
    // Validate inputs
    if (!ethers.utils.isAddress(walletAddress)) {
      throw new Error('Invalid wallet address');
    }
    
    if (!validator.isAlphanumeric(username, 'en-US', { ignore: '_-' })) {
      throw new Error('Invalid username format');
    }
    
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const sql = `
        INSERT INTO users (wallet_address, username, email, created_at)
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
      `;
      
      db.run(sql, [
        walletAddress.toLowerCase(),
        username,
        email || null
      ], function(err) {
        if (err) {
          if (err.code === 'SQLITE_CONSTRAINT_UNIQUE') {
            reject(new Error('User already exists'));
          } else {
            logSecurityEvent('database_error', err);
            reject(err);
          }
        } else {
          resolve({ id: this.lastID });
        }
      });
    });
  }
}


ğŸ“ Data Protection & Privacy

GDPR/RODO Compliance

Data Minimization
Zbieramy tylko niezbÄ™dne dane:
Wallet Address: Do identyfikacji uÅ¼ytkownika
Username: Do publicznej identyfikacji
Email: Opcjonalny, tylko dla notyfikacji
Profile Data: Tylko to co uÅ¼ytkownik Å›wiadomie udostÄ™pnia

User Rights Implementation
typescript
// GDPR user rights API
export class GDPRCompliance {
  // Right to Access (Art. 15)
  static async exportUserData(userId: string): Promise<UserDataExport> {
    const user = await db.getUserById(userId);
    const profile = await db.getArtistProfile(userId);
    const nfts = await db.getUserNFTs(userId);
    const transactions = await db.getUserTransactions(userId);
    
    return {
      personalData: {
        username: user.username,
        email: user.email,
        createdAt: user.created_at
      },
      profileData: profile,
      nftData: nfts.map(nft => ({
        title: nft.title,
        description: nft.description,
        createdAt: nft.created_at
      })),
      transactionData: transactions.map(tx => ({
        type: tx.type,
        amount: tx.amount,
        timestamp: tx.timestamp
      }))
    };
  }
  
  // Right to Erasure (Art. 17)
  static async deleteUserData(userId: string): Promise<void> {
    await db.transaction(async (trx) => {
      // Anonymize instead of delete for blockchain integrity
      await trx('users').where('id', userId).update({
        email: null,
        username: deleted_user_${userId},
        bio: null,
        deleted_at: new Date()
      });
      
      // Remove personal content
      await trx('artist_profiles').where('user_id', userId).update({
        bio: null,
        social_links: null
      });
      
      // Mark NFTs as from deleted user
      await trx('nfts').where('creator_id', userId).update({
        creator_id: null,
        creator_name: 'Deleted User'
      });
    });
  }
  
  // Right to Rectification (Art. 16)
  static async updateUserData(userId: string, updates: UserDataUpdate): Promise<void> {
    // Validate updates
    const schema = Joi.object({
      username: Joi.string().min(3).max(50).optional(),
      email: Joi.string().email().allow(null).optional(),
      bio: Joi.string().max(1000).allow(null).optional()
    });
    
    const { error, value } = schema.validate(updates);
    if (error) {
      throw new Error(Invalid update data: ${error.message});
    }
    
    await db.updateUser(userId, value);
  }
}


Data Encryption

At Rest Encryption
javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');

class DataEncryption {
  static encrypt(text, key) {
    const iv = crypto.randomBytes(16);
    const cipher = crypto.createCipher('aes-256-gcm', key, iv);
    
    let encrypted = cipher.update(text, 'utf8', 'hex');
    encrypted += cipher.final('hex');
    
    const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
    
    return {
      encrypted,
      iv: iv.toString('hex'),
      authTag: authTag.toString('hex')
    };
  }
  
  static decrypt(encryptedData, key) {
    const decipher = crypto.createDecipher('aes-256-gcm', key, 
      Buffer.from(encryptedData.iv, 'hex'));
    
    decipher.setAuthTag(Buffer.from(encryptedData.authTag, 'hex'));
    
    let decrypted = decipher.update(encryptedData.encrypted, 'hex', 'utf8');
    decrypted += decipher.final('utf8');
    
    return decrypted;
  }
}

// Encrypt sensitive data before storage
async function storeSensitiveData(userId, data) {
  const encryptionKey = process.env.DATA_ENCRYPTION_KEY;
  const encrypted = DataEncryption.encrypt(JSON.stringify(data), encryptionKey);
  
  await db.run(`
    INSERT INTO encrypted_data (user_id, encrypted_content, iv, auth_tag)
    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
  `, [userId, encrypted.encrypted, encrypted.iv, encrypted.authTag]);
}


ğŸ” Security Monitoring

Real-time Threat Detection

Anomaly Detection
typescript
class SecurityMonitor {
  private static suspiciousPatterns = [
    /script\s*:/i,
    /<iframe/i,
    /javascript:/i,
    /vbscript:/i,
    /onload=/i,
    /onerror=/i
  ];
  
  static detectXSSAttempt(input: string): boolean {
    return this.suspiciousPatterns.some(pattern => pattern.test(input));
  }
  
  static async logSecurityEvent(
    eventType: string, 
    details: any, 
    severity: 'low' | 'medium' | 'high' | 'critical' = 'medium'
  ): Promise<void> {
    const event = {
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      type: eventType,
      severity,
      details,
      ip: this.getClientIP(),
      userAgent: this.getUserAgent()
    };
    
    // Store in database
    await db.run(`
      INSERT INTO security_events (type, severity, details, ip, user_agent, timestamp)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
    `, [
      event.type,
      event.severity,
      JSON.stringify(event.details),
      event.ip,
      event.userAgent,
      event.timestamp
    ]);
    
    // Alert for critical events
    if (severity === 'critical') {
      await this.sendSecurityAlert(event);
    }
  }
  
  private static async sendSecurityAlert(event: SecurityEvent): Promise<void> {
    // Webhook do security team
    await fetch(process.env.SECURITY_WEBHOOK_URL, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        text: ğŸš¨ Security Alert: ${event.type},
        attachments: [{
          color: 'danger',
          fields: [
            { title: 'Severity', value: event.severity, short: true },
            { title: 'IP', value: event.ip, short: true },
            { title: 'Details', value: JSON.stringify(event.details, null, 2) }
          ]
        }]
      })
    });
  }
}


Smart Contract Monitoring
typescript
// Monitor smart contract events for suspicious activity
class ContractMonitor {
  static async startMonitoring() {
    const contract = new ethers.Contract(CONTRACT_ADDRESS, ABI, provider);
    
    // Monitor large transfers
    contract.on('Transfer', async (from, to, tokenId, event) => {
      // Check for suspicious patterns
      if (await this.isFlashLoanAttack(event)) {
        await SecurityMonitor.logSecurityEvent('potential_flash_loan_attack', {
          from, to, tokenId, txHash: event.transactionHash
        }, 'critical');
      }
      
      // Check for rapid successive transfers
      if (await this.isRapidTransfer(from, to)) {
        await SecurityMonitor.logSecurityEvent('rapid_transfer_detected', {
          from, to, tokenId
        }, 'medium');
      }
    });
    
    // Monitor failed transactions
    provider.on('pending', async (txHash) => {
      try {
        const tx = await provider.getTransaction(txHash);
        if (tx.to === CONTRACT_ADDRESS) {
          const receipt = await tx.wait();
          if (receipt.status === 0) {
            await SecurityMonitor.logSecurityEvent('contract_call_failed', {
              txHash, from: tx.from, gasUsed: receipt.gasUsed
            }, 'low');
          }
        }
      } catch (error) {
        // Handle monitoring errors
      }
    });
  }
  
  private static async isFlashLoanAttack(event): Promise<boolean> {
    // Detect rapid buy-sell patterns within same block
    const block = await provider.getBlock(event.blockNumber);
    const blockTransactions = await Promise.all(
      block.transactions.map(txHash => provider.getTransaction(txHash))
    );
    
    const contractTransactions = blockTransactions.filter(tx => tx.to === CONTRACT_ADDRESS);
    return contractTransactions.length > 10; // Suspicious if >10 contract calls in one block
  }
}


ğŸš¨ Incident Response

Security Incident Playbook

Severity Levels
1. Low: Pojedyncze prÃ³by atakÃ³w, automatycznie zablokowane
2. Medium: Wykryte wzorce atakÃ³w, wymagana analiza
3. High: Aktywny atak w toku, wymagana natychmiastowa akcja
4. Critical: Naruszenie bezpieczeÅ„stwa, potencjalna utrata Å›rodkÃ³w

Response Procedures

Critical Incident Response
typescript
class IncidentResponse {
  static async handleCriticalIncident(incident: SecurityIncident): Promise<void> {
    // 1. Immediate containment
    await this.enableEmergencyMode();
    
    // 2. Pause all critical operations
    await this.pauseSmartContracts();
    
    // 3. Notify security team
    await this.notifySecurityTeam(incident);
    
    // 4. Begin investigation
    await this.startInvestigation(incident);
    
    // 5. Communicate with users
    await this.notifyUsers('Service temporarily paused for security review');
  }
  
  private static async enableEmergencyMode(): Promise<void> {
    // Activate emergency circuit breaker
    await redis.set('emergency_mode', 'true', 'EX', 3600); // 1 hour
    
    // Block new transactions
    await redis.set('transactions_blocked', 'true', 'EX', 3600);
    
    // Enable enhanced monitoring
    await redis.set('enhanced_monitoring', 'true', 'EX', 3600);
  }
  
  private static async pauseSmartContracts(): Promise<void> {
    const emergencyWallet = new ethers.Wallet(
      process.env.EMERGENCY_PRIVATE_KEY, 
      provider
    );
    
    const contracts = [
      new ethers.Contract(NFT_CONTRACT_ADDRESS, NFT_ABI, emergencyWallet),
      new ethers.Contract(TOKEN_CONTRACT_ADDRESS, TOKEN_ABI, emergencyWallet),
      new ethers.Contract(MARKETPLACE_CONTRACT_ADDRESS, MARKETPLACE_ABI, emergencyWallet)
    ];
    
    for (const contract of contracts) {
      try {
        if (contract.pause) {
          await contract.pause();
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(Failed to pause contract ${contract.address}:, error);
      }
    }
  }
}


Recovery Procedures

Post-Incident Recovery
1. Vulnerability Assessment: PeÅ‚na analiza przyczyn
2. Patch Development: Szybkie poprawki bezpieczeÅ„stwa
3. Testing: Thorough testing w Å›rodowisku testowym
4. Gradual Restoration: Stopniowe przywracanie funkcji
5. Post-Mortem: Analiza incydentu i ulepszenia

ğŸ“‹ Security Checklist

Pre-Launch Security Audit

Smart Contracts
[ ] Wszystkie kontrakty audytowane przez zewnÄ™trznÄ… firmÄ™
[ ] Implementacja emergency pause mechanism
[ ] Reentrancy protection na wszystkich zewnÄ™trznych wywoÅ‚aniach
[ ] Access control dla wszystkich admin functions
[ ] Rate limiting dla user-facing functions
[ ] Input validation dla wszystkich parametrÃ³w
[ ] Event emission dla wszystkich krytycznych operacji

Backend API
[ ] Rate limiting na wszystkich endpoints
[ ] Input validation i sanitization
[ ] SQL injection protection (parameterized queries)
[ ] CORS properly configured
[ ] HTTPS enforced w produkcji
[ ] Authentication i authorization na wszystkich chronionych routes
[ ] Sensitive data encryption at rest
[ ] Proper error handling (nie wycieka internal details)

Frontend
[ ] Content Security Policy headers
[ ] XSS protection przez input sanitization
[ ] Secure authentication token handling
[ ] HTTPS-only cookies w produkcji
[ ] No sensitive data w localStorage
[ ] Proper logout implementation
[ ] Input validation przed wysÅ‚aniem do backend

Infrastructure
[ ] Database access restricted do aplikacji
[ ] Environment variables properly secured
[ ] Regular security updates dla wszystkich dependencies
[ ] Monitoring i alerting system
[ ] Backup i disaster recovery plan
[ ] Penetration testing completed

Ongoing Security Maintenance

Daily Tasks
[ ] Review security logs i alerts
[ ] Monitor transaction patterns dla anomalii
[ ] Check for dependency updates z security fixes
[ ] Verify backup systems dziaÅ‚ajÄ…

Weekly Tasks
[ ] Security metrics review
[ ] Incident response training
[ ] Update security documentation
[ ] Review user reports dla security issues

Monthly Tasks
[ ] Penetration testing
[ ] Security architecture review
[ ] Update incident response procedures
[ ] Team security training

ğŸ”’ Web3 & Blockchain Security

Smart Contract Security

Audited Contracts
Wszystkie nasze smart contracts przeszÅ‚y audyt bezpieczeÅ„stwa:

solidity
// PrzykÅ‚ad zabezpieczonego kontraktu NFT
pragma solidity ^0.8.19;

import "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC721/ERC721.sol";
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/security/ReentrancyGuard.sol";
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";

contract SecureHipHopNFT is ERC721, ReentrancyGuard, Ownable {
    using SafeMath for uint256;
    
    // Reentrancy protection
    modifier nonReentrant() {
        require(!_locked, "Reentrant call");
        _locked = true;
        _;
        _locked = false;
    }
    
    // Rate limiting per user
    mapping(address => uint256) private _lastMintTime;
    uint256 private constant MINT_COOLDOWN = 300; // 5 minutes
    
    function safeMint(address to, string memory uri) 
        public 
        nonReentrant 
        onlyOwner 
    {
        require(
            block.timestamp >= _lastMintTime[to] + MINT_COOLDOWN,
            "Mint cooldown active"
        );
        
        _lastMintTime[to] = block.timestamp;
        uint256 tokenId = _tokenIdCounter.current();
        _tokenIdCounter.increment();
        _safeMint(to, tokenId);
        _setTokenURI(tokenId, uri);
    }
}

Connection Security
typescript
// Bezpieczne poÅ‚Ä…czenie z portfelem
export async function connectWallet(): Promise<WalletConnection> {
  try {
    // SprawdÅº czy portfel jest dostÄ™pny
    if (!window.ethereum) {
      throw new Error('No Web3 wallet detected');
    }
    
    // Request connection z timeout
    const accounts = await Promise.race([
      window.ethereum.request({ 
        method: 'eth_requestAccounts' 
      }),
      new Promise((_, reject) => 
        setTimeout(() => reject(new Error('Connection timeout')), 10000)
      )
    ]);
    
    // SprawdÅº network
    const chainId = await window.ethereum.request({ 
      method: 'eth_chainId' 
    });
    
    if (chainId !== POLYGON_CHAIN_ID) {
      await switchToPolygon();
    }
    
    // Waliduj adres
    const address = accounts[0];
    if (!ethers.utils.isAddress(address)) {
      throw new Error('Invalid wallet address');
    }
    
    return {
      address: address.toLowerCase(),
      chainId,
      connected: true
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    logSecurityEvent('wallet_connection_failed', error);
    throw error;
  }
}


Transaction Security

Secure Transaction Flow
1. Frontend Validation: Basic input validation
2. Backend Verification: Server-side double-check
3. Smart Contract Validation: Final on-chain validation
4. Event Monitoring: Real-time fraud detection

Gas Optimization & Protection
typescript
// Secure transaction handling
export async function executeSecureTransaction(
  contractMethod: ContractMethod,
  params: any[],
  options: TransactionOptions = {}
): Promise<TransactionResult> {
  
  // Estimate gas with safety margin
  const estimatedGas = await contractMethod.estimateGas(...params);
  const gasLimit = estimatedGas.mul(120).div(100); // 20% buffer
  
  // Check gas price isn't excessive
  const gasPrice = await provider.getGasPrice();
  const maxGasPrice = ethers.utils.parseUnits('100', 'gwei');
  
  if (gasPrice.gt(maxGasPrice)) {
    throw new Error('Gas price too high, try again later');
  }
  
  // Execute with timeout
  const tx = await contractMethod(...params, {
    gasLimit,
    gasPrice,
    ...options
  });
  
  // Monitor transaction
  const receipt = await tx.wait(2); // Wait for 2 confirmations
  
  return {
    hash: tx.hash,
    receipt,
    confirmed: receipt.confirmations >= 2
  };
}

XSS Protection
typescript
// Input sanitization
import DOMPurify from 'dompurify';

export function sanitizeUserInput(input: string): string {
  // Remove dangerous HTML
  const clean = DOMPurify.sanitize(input, {
    ALLOWED_TAGS: ['b', 'i', 'em', 'strong', 'br'],
    ALLOWED_ATTR: []
  });
  
  // Additional validation
  if (clean.length > 1000) {
    throw new Error('Input too long');
  }
  
  return clean;
}

// Safe rendering
export function SafeUserContent({ content }: { content: string }) {
  const sanitized = sanitizeUserInput(content);
  
  return (
    <div 
      dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: sanitized }}
      className="user-content"
    />
  );
}


Authentication Security
typescript
// JWT token handling
export class SecureAuth {
  private static readonly TOKEN_KEY = 'hip_hop_token';
  private static readonly REFRESH_KEY = 'hip_hop_refresh';
  
  static storeTokens(accessToken: string, refreshToken: string): void {
    // Use httpOnly cookies in production
    const secure = process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production';
    
    document.cookie = ${this.TOKEN_KEY}=${accessToken}; secure=${secure}; samesite=strict; max-age=900; // 15 min
    document.cookie = ${this.REFRESH_KEY}=${refreshToken}; secure=${secure}; samesite=strict; max-age=604800; // 7 days
  }
  
  static async refreshToken(): Promise<string> {
    const refreshToken = this.getRefreshToken();
    if (!refreshToken) {
      throw new Error('No refresh token available');
    }
    
    const response = await fetch('/api/auth/refresh', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ refreshToken })
    });
    
    if (!response.ok) {
      this.clearTokens();
      throw new Error('Token refresh failed');
    }
    
    const { accessToken, refreshToken: newRefreshToken } = await response.json();
    this.storeTokens(accessToken, newRefreshToken);
    
    return accessToken;
  }
}


Backend Security

API Security
javascript
// Rate limiting
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');

const createRateLimit = (windowMs, max, message) => rateLimit({
  windowMs,
  max,
  message: { error: message },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  handler: (req, res) => {
    logSecurityEvent('rate_limit_exceeded', {
      ip: req.ip,
      path: req.path,
      userAgent: req.get('User-Agent')
    });
    res.status(429).json({ error: message });
  }
});

// Different limits for different endpoints
app.use('/api/auth/', createRateLimit(15 * 60 * 1000, 5, 'Too many auth attempts'));
app.use('/api/mint/', createRateLimit(60 * 1000, 3, 'Too many mint requests'));
app.use('/api/', createRateLimit(15 * 60 * 1000, 100, 'Too many requests'));


Input Validation
javascript
const Joi = require('joi');
const validator = require('validator');

// Schema validation
const userProfileSchema = Joi.object({
  stageName: Joi.string().min(3).max(50).pattern(/^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+$/).required(),
  bio: Joi.string().max(1000).optional(),
  email: Joi.string().email().optional(),
  socialLinks: Joi.object({
    twitter: Joi.string().uri().optional(),
    instagram: Joi.string().uri().optional(),
    youtube: Joi.string().uri().optional()
  }).optional()
});

// Validation middleware
function validateInput(schema) {
  return (req, res, next) => {
    const { error, value } = schema.validate(req.body);
    
    if (error) {
      logSecurityEvent('validation_failed', {
        error: error.details[0].message,
        path: req.path,
        ip: req.ip
      });
      
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: 'Invalid input',
        details: error.details[0].message
      });
    }
    
    // Sanitize
    req.body = sanitizeObject(value);
    next();
  };
}

function sanitizeObject(obj) {
  const sanitized = {};
  
  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {
    if (typeof value === 'string') {
      sanitized[key] = validator.escape(value.trim());
    } else if (typeof value === 'object' && value !== null) {
      sanitized[key] = sanitizeObject(value);
    } else {
      sanitized[key] = value;
    }
  }
  
  return sanitized;
}


SQL Injection Prevention
javascript
// Parameterized queries only
const db = require('sqlite3').verbose();

class SecureDatabase {
  static async getUserByWallet(walletAddress) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      // NEVER use string concatenation
      const sql = `
        SELECT id, username, email, created_at 
        FROM users 
        WHERE wallet_address = ? AND active = 1
      `;
      
      db.get(sql, [walletAddress.toLowerCase()], (err, row) => {
        if (err) {
          logSecurityEvent('database_error', err);
          reject(err);
        } else {
          resolve(row);
        }
      });
    });
  }
  
  static async createUser(userData) {
    const { walletAddress, username, email } = userData;
    
    // Validate inputs
    if (!ethers.utils.isAddress(walletAddress)) {
      throw new Error('Invalid wallet address');
    }
    
    if (!validator.isAlphanumeric(username, 'en-US', { ignore: '_-' })) {
      throw new Error('Invalid username format');
    }
    
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const sql = `
        INSERT INTO users (wallet_address, username, email, created_at)
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
      `;
      
      db.run(sql, [
        walletAddress.toLowerCase(),
        username,
        email || null
      ], function(err) {
        if (err) {
          if (err.code === 'SQLITE_CONSTRAINT_UNIQUE') {
            reject(new Error('User already exists'));
          } else {
            logSecurityEvent('database_error', err);
            reject(err);
          }
        } else {
          resolve({ id: this.lastID });
        }
      });
    });
  }
}

Data Minimization

Username: Do publicznej identyfikacji
Email: Opcjonalny, tylko dla notyfikacji
Profile Data: Tylko to co uÅ¼ytkownik Å›wiadomie udostÄ™pnia

User Rights Implementation
typescript
// GDPR user rights API
export class GDPRCompliance {
  // Right to Access (Art. 15)
  static async exportUserData(userId: string): Promise<UserDataExport> {
    const user = await db.getUserById(userId);
    const profile = await db.getArtistProfile(userId);
    const nfts = await db.getUserNFTs(userId);
    const transactions = await db.getUserTransactions(userId);
    
    return {
      personalData: {
        username: user.username,
        email: user.email,
        createdAt: user.created_at
      },
      profileData: profile,
      nftData: nfts.map(nft => ({
        title: nft.title,
        description: nft.description,
        createdAt: nft.created_at
      })),
      transactionData: transactions.map(tx => ({
        type: tx.type,
        amount: tx.amount,
        timestamp: tx.timestamp
      }))
    };
  }
  
  // Right to Erasure (Art. 17)
  static async deleteUserData(userId: string): Promise<void> {
    await db.transaction(async (trx) => {
      // Anonymize instead of delete for blockchain integrity
      await trx('users').where('id', userId).update({
        email: null,
        username: deleted_user_${userId},
        bio: null,
        deleted_at: new Date()
      });
      
      // Remove personal content
      await trx('artist_profiles').where('user_id', userId).update({
        bio: null,
        social_links: null
      });
      
      // Mark NFTs as from deleted user
      await trx('nfts').where('creator_id', userId).update({
        creator_id: null,
        creator_name: 'Deleted User'
      });
    });
  }
  
  // Right to Rectification (Art. 16)
  static async updateUserData(userId: string, updates: UserDataUpdate): Promise<void> {
    // Validate updates
    const schema = Joi.object({
      username: Joi.string().min(3).max(50).optional(),
      email: Joi.string().email().allow(null).optional(),
      bio: Joi.string().max(1000).allow(null).optional()
    });
    
    const { error, value } = schema.validate(updates);
    if (error) {
      throw new Error(Invalid update data: ${error.message});
    }
    
    await db.updateUser(userId, value);
  }
}


Data Encryption

At Rest Encryption
javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');

class DataEncryption {
  static encrypt(text, key) {
    const iv = crypto.randomBytes(16);
    const cipher = crypto.createCipher('aes-256-gcm', key, iv);
    
    let encrypted = cipher.update(text, 'utf8', 'hex');
    encrypted += cipher.final('hex');
    
    const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
    
    return {
      encrypted,
      iv: iv.toString('hex'),
      authTag: authTag.toString('hex')
    };
  }
  
  static decrypt(encryptedData, key) {
    const decipher = crypto.createDecipher('aes-256-gcm', key, 
      Buffer.from(encryptedData.iv, 'hex'));
    
    decipher.setAuthTag(Buffer.from(encryptedData.authTag, 'hex'));
    
    let decrypted = decipher.update(encryptedData.encrypted, 'hex', 'utf8');
    decrypted += decipher.final('utf8');
    
    return decrypted;
  }
}

// Encrypt sensitive data before storage
async function storeSensitiveData(userId, data) {
  const encryptionKey = process.env.DATA_ENCRYPTION_KEY;
  const encrypted = DataEncryption.encrypt(JSON.stringify(data), encryptionKey);
  
  await db.run(`
    INSERT INTO encrypted_data (user_id, encrypted_content, iv, auth_tag)
    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
  `, [userId, encrypted.encrypted, encrypted.iv, encrypted.authTag]);
}


ğŸ” Security Monitoring

Real-time Threat Detection

Anomaly Detection
typescript
class SecurityMonitor {
  private static suspiciousPatterns = [
    /script\s*:/i,
    /<iframe/i,
    /javascript:/i,
    /vbscript:/i,
    /onload=/i,
    /onerror=/i
  ];
  
  static detectXSSAttempt(input: string): boolean {
    return this.suspiciousPatterns.some(pattern => pattern.test(input));
  }
  
  static async logSecurityEvent(
    eventType: string, 
    details: any, 
    severity: 'low' | 'medium' | 'high' | 'critical' = 'medium'
  ): Promise<void> {
    const event = {
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      type: eventType,
      severity,
      details,
      ip: this.getClientIP(),
      userAgent: this.getUserAgent()
    };
    
    // Store in database
    await db.run(`
      INSERT INTO security_events (type, severity, details, ip, user_agent, timestamp)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
    `, [
      event.type,
      event.severity,
      JSON.stringify(event.details),
      event.ip,
      event.userAgent,
      event.timestamp
    ]);
    
    // Alert for critical events
    if (severity === 'critical') {
      await this.sendSecurityAlert(event);
    }
  }
  
  private static async sendSecurityAlert(event: SecurityEvent): Promise<void> {
    // Webhook do security team
    await fetch(process.env.SECURITY_WEBHOOK_URL, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        text: ğŸš¨ Security Alert: ${event.type},
        attachments: [{
          color: 'danger',
          fields: [
            { title: 'Severity', value: event.severity, short: true },
            { title: 'IP', value: event.ip, short: true },
            { title: 'Details', value: JSON.stringify(event.details, null, 2) }
          ]
        }]
      })
    });
  }
}


Smart Contract Monitoring
typescript
// Monitor smart contract events for suspicious activity
class ContractMonitor {
  static async startMonitoring() {
    const contract = new ethers.Contract(CONTRACT_ADDRESS, ABI, provider);
    
    // Monitor large transfers
    contract.on('Transfer', async (from, to, tokenId, event) => {
      // Check for suspicious patterns
      if (await this.isFlashLoanAttack(event)) {
        await SecurityMonitor.logSecurityEvent('potential_flash_loan_attack', {
          from, to, tokenId, txHash: event.transactionHash
        }, 'critical');
      }
      
      // Check for rapid successive transfers
      if (await this.isRapidTransfer(from, to)) {
        await SecurityMonitor.logSecurityEvent('rapid_transfer_detected', {
          from, to, tokenId
        }, 'medium');
      }
    });
    
    // Monitor failed transactions
    provider.on('pending', async (txHash) => {
      try {
        const tx = await provider.getTransaction(txHash);
        if (tx.to === CONTRACT_ADDRESS) {
          const receipt = await tx.wait();
          if (receipt.status === 0) {
            await SecurityMonitor.logSecurityEvent('contract_call_failed', {
              txHash, from: tx.from, gasUsed: receipt.gasUsed
            }, 'low');
          }
        }
      } catch (error) {
        // Handle monitoring errors
      }
    });
  }
  
  private static async isFlashLoanAttack(event): Promise<boolean> {
    // Detect rapid buy-sell patterns within same block
    const block = await provider.getBlock(event.blockNumber);
    const blockTransactions = await Promise.all(
      block.transactions.map(txHash => provider.getTransaction(txHash))
    );
    
    const contractTransactions = blockTransactions.filter(tx => tx.to === CONTRACT_ADDRESS);
    return contractTransactions.length > 10; // Suspicious if >10 contract calls in one block
  }
}


ğŸš¨ Incident Response

Security Incident Playbook

Severity Levels
1. Low: Pojedyncze prÃ³by atakÃ³w, automatycznie zablokowane
2. Medium: Wykryte wzorce atakÃ³w, wymagana analiza
3. High: Aktywny atak w toku, wymagana natychmiastowa akcja
4. Critical: Naruszenie bezpieczeÅ„stwa, potencjalna utrata Å›rodkÃ³w

Response Procedures

Critical Incident Response
typescript
class IncidentResponse {
  static async handleCriticalIncident(incident: SecurityIncident): Promise<void> {
    // 1. Immediate containment
    await this.enableEmergencyMode();
    
    // 2. Pause all critical operations
    await this.pauseSmartContracts();
    
    // 3. Notify security team
    await this.notifySecurityTeam(incident);
    
    // 4. Begin investigation
    await this.startInvestigation(incident);
    
    // 5. Communicate with users
    await this.notifyUsers('Service temporarily paused for security review');
  }
  
  private static async enableEmergencyMode(): Promise<void> {
    // Activate emergency circuit breaker
    await redis.set('emergency_mode', 'true', 'EX', 3600); // 1 hour
    
    // Block new transactions
    await redis.set('transactions_blocked', 'true', 'EX', 3600);
    
    // Enable enhanced monitoring
    await redis.set('enhanced_monitoring', 'true', 'EX', 3600);
  }
  
  private static async pauseSmartContracts(): Promise<void> {
    const emergencyWallet = new ethers.Wallet(
      process.env.EMERGENCY_PRIVATE_KEY, 
      provider
    );
    
    const contracts = [
      new ethers.Contract(NFT_CONTRACT_ADDRESS, NFT_ABI, emergencyWallet),
      new ethers.Contract(TOKEN_CONTRACT_ADDRESS, TOKEN_ABI, emergencyWallet),
      new ethers.Contract(MARKETPLACE_CONTRACT_ADDRESS, MARKETPLACE_ABI, emergencyWallet)
    ];
    
    for (const contract of contracts) {
      try {
        if (contract.pause) {
          await contract.pause();
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(Failed to pause contract ${contract.address}:, error);
      }
    }
  }
}


Recovery Procedures

Post-Incident Recovery
1. Vulnerability Assessment: PeÅ‚na analiza przyczyn
2. Patch Development: Szybkie poprawki bezpieczeÅ„stwa
3. Testing: Thorough testing w Å›rodowisku testowym
4. Gradual Restoration: Stopniowe przywracanie funkcji
5. Post-Mortem: Analiza incydentu i ulepszenia

Hip-Hop Universe + Rocket Fuell Girls Integration

ğŸ¯ Executive Summary

This document outlines critical security measures, compliance requirements, and legal considerations for the integrated Hip-Hop Universe + Rocket Fuell Girls platform.

âš ï¸ CRITICAL SECURITY ISSUES IDENTIFIED

1. Adult Content Compliance - PRIORITY 1

Rocket Fuell Girls contains "erotics-fantasies" section
No age verification system implemented
Missing consent management system
No DMCA takedown procedures

// Age verification implementation required
const ageVerificationMiddleware = (req, res, next) => {
    const ageVerified = req.session.ageVerified || req.cookies.ageVerified;
    
    if (!ageVerified && req.path.includes('/fantasy')) {
        return res.redirect('/age-verification');
    }
    next();
};

// Consent tracking system
const consentSchema = {

const clamscan = require('clamscan');
const clam = await new clamscan().init();

const scanFile = async (buffer) => {
    const result = await clam.scanBuffer(buffer);
    if (!result.isClean) {
        throw new Error('File contains malware');
    }
    return result;
};

// Content moderation with AI
const moderateImage = async (imageBuffer) => {
    const response = await fetch('https://api.sightengine.com/1.0/check.json', {
        method: 'POST',

    });
    
    const moderation = await response.json();

3. Authentication Security - PRIORITY 2

Enhancements Needed:
javascript
// Account lockout after failed attempts
const MAX_LOGIN_ATTEMPTS = 5;
const LOCKOUT_TIME = 15 * 60 * 1000; // 15 minutes

const checkAccountLockout = async (username) => {
    const attempts = await redis.get(login_attempts:${username});
    if (attempts >= MAX_LOGIN_ATTEMPTS) {
        const lockoutExpiry = await redis.ttl(login_attempts:${username});
        throw new Error(Account locked for ${lockoutExpiry} seconds);
    }
};

// 2FA implementation
const generateTOTP = (secret) => {
    return speakeasy.totp({ secret, encoding: 'base32' });
};

    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,

    request_type VARCHAR(50), -- 'deletion', 'export', 'correction'
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'pending',
    requested_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    processed_at TIMESTAMP,

2. DMCA Compliance (US Copyright)
Status: âŒ NOT IMPLEMENTED

Required Elements:
[ ] DMCA agent designation
[ ] Takedown request form
[ ] Counter-notification process
[ ] Repeat infringer policy

javascript
// DMCA takedown endpoint
router.post('/dmca/takedown', async (req, res) => {
    const { assetId, claimantInfo, copyrightWork, infringementClaim } = req.body;
    
    // Validate DMCA request
    if (!isValidDMCARequest(req.body)) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid DMCA request' });
    }
    
    // Immediately disable asset
    await pool.query('UPDATE media_assets SET status = \'dmca_disabled\' WHERE id = $1', [assetId]);
    
    // Notify asset owner
    await sendDMCANotification(assetId, claimantInfo);
    
    res.json({ success: true, case_id: generateCaseId() });
});


3. Age Verification (18+ Content)
Status: âš ï¸ BASIC IMPLEMENTATION

Current: Simple yes/no verification
Required: Enhanced verification

javascript
// Enhanced age verification
const verifyAge = async (req, res) => {
    const { birthDate, idDocument, country } = req.body;
    
    // Calculate age
    const age = calculateAge(birthDate);
    if (age < 18) {
        return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Must be 18 or older' });
    }
    
    // Store verification record
    await pool.query(`
        INSERT INTO age_verifications (user_id, birth_date, verification_method, country, ip_address)
        VALUES ($1, $2, 'self_declared', $3, $4)
    `, [req.user.id, birthDate, country, req.ip]);
    
    // Set long-term verification cookie
    res.cookie('age_verified', 'true', { 
        maxAge: 365 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000, // 1 year
        httpOnly: true,
        secure: true,
        sameSite: 'strict'
    });
};

// Emergency content disable
const emergencyDisable = async (assetId, reason) => {
    await pool.query(`

        SET status = 'emergency_disabled', 
            disabled_reason = $1,
            disabled_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP

    `, [reason, assetId]);

};

Hip-Hop Universe + Rocket Fuell Girls Integration

ğŸ¯ Executive Summary

This document outlines critical security measures, compliance requirements, and legal considerations for the integrated Hip-Hop Universe + Rocket Fuell Girls platform.

âš ï¸ CRITICAL SECURITY ISSUES IDENTIFIED

1. Adult Content Compliance - PRIORITY 1
Risk Level: CRITICAL

Issues:
Rocket Fuell Girls contains "erotics-fantasies" section
No age verification system implemented
Missing consent management system
No DMCA takedown procedures

Required Actions:
javascript
// Age verification implementation required
const ageVerificationMiddleware = (req, res, next) => {
    const ageVerified = req.session.ageVerified || req.cookies.ageVerified;
    
    if (!ageVerified && req.path.includes('/fantasy')) {
        return res.redirect('/age-verification');
    }
    next();
};

// Consent tracking system
const consentSchema = {
    userId: 'INTEGER',
    consentType: 'VARCHAR(50)', // 'age_verification', 'content_usage', 'data_processing'
    consentGiven: 'BOOLEAN',
    ipAddress: 'INET',
    timestamp: 'TIMESTAMP',
    evidence: 'TEXT' // Screenshot, form data, etc.
};


2. File Upload Security - PRIORITY 1
Risk Level: HIGH

Current Status: âš ï¸ Partially Implemented
âœ… EXIF removal (Sharp.js)
âœ… File type validation
âœ… Size limits (8MB)
âŒ Virus scanning
âŒ Content moderation AI
âŒ Watermarking

Enhanced Security Implementation:
javascript
// Add ClamAV virus scanning
const clamscan = require('clamscan');
const clam = await new clamscan().init();

const scanFile = async (buffer) => {
    const result = await clam.scanBuffer(buffer);
    if (!result.isClean) {
        throw new Error('File contains malware');
    }
    return result;
};

// Content moderation with AI
const moderateImage = async (imageBuffer) => {
    const response = await fetch('https://api.sightengine.com/1.0/check.json', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: formData
    });
    
    const moderation = await response.json();
    
    if (moderation.nudity.sexual_display > 0.8) {
        return { approved: false, reason: 'Explicit content detected' };
    }
    
    return { approved: true };
};

ğŸ› ï¸ Stos Technologiczny

Frontend
Framework: Next.js 14 + React 18
Styling: Tailwind CSS + Framer Motion
State Management: Zustand + React Query
UI Components: Radix UI + Custom Design System
Web3: ethers.js + web3modal + RainbowKit

Backend
API: Node.js + Express + GraphQL
Database: PostgreSQL (relacyjne) + Redis (cache)
Authentication: Auth0 + Web3 wallets (MetaMask/WalletConnect)
File Storage: IPFS (Pinata) + AWS S3
CDN: Cloudflare

Blockchain
Network: Polygon (Ethereum L2)
Smart Contracts: Solidity + Hardhat
Tokens: 
ERC-20 (DRT Token)
ERC-721/1155 (Consciousness NFTs)
Development: Hardhat + OpenZeppelin

AI/ML
Recommendations: GPT-4 API (prototyp)
Style Analysis: TensorFlow.js
Content Moderation: AWS Rekognition
Custom Models: Python + scikit-learn

DevOps & Monitoring
CI/CD: GitHub Actions
Hosting: Vercel (frontend) + AWS/DigitalOcean (backend)
Monitoring: Sentry + Prometheus/Grafana
Analytics: LogRocket + Custom event tracking

ğŸ“‹ Modele Danych (PostgreSQL)

Core Tables
sql
-- UÅ¼ytkownicy
CREATE TABLE users (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    display_name VARCHAR(100),
    wallet_address VARCHAR(42),
    bio TEXT,
    avatar_uri VARCHAR(500),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Profile artystÃ³w
CREATE TABLE artists (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    stage_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    genre VARCHAR(50),
    social_links JSONB,
    verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    metadata_uri VARCHAR(500),
    consciousness_profile_id INTEGER
);

-- Utwory/Beaty
CREATE TABLE tracks (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    artist_id INTEGER REFERENCES artists(id),
    title VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    ipfs_uri VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    preview_uri VARCHAR(500),
    price_drt DECIMAL(18,8),
    price_usd DECIMAL(10,2),
    license_type VARCHAR(50),
    is_nft BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    token_id INTEGER,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- NFT
CREATE TABLE nfts (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    token_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    contract_address VARCHAR(42) NOT NULL,
    owner_address VARCHAR(42) NOT NULL,
    creator_address VARCHAR(42) NOT NULL,
    metadata_uri VARCHAR(500),
    consciousness_data JSONB,
    minted_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    last_transfer_at TIMESTAMP
);

-- Transakcje
CREATE TABLE transactions (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    tx_hash VARCHAR(66),
    type VARCHAR(50), -- 'purchase', 'mint', 'transfer', 'royalty'
    amount_drt DECIMAL(18,8),
    amount_usd DECIMAL(10,2),
    status VARCHAR(20), -- 'pending', 'completed', 'failed'
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Profile Å›wiadomoÅ›ci
CREATE TABLE consciousness_profiles (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    owner_id INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    vector_data JSONB, -- Zaszyfrowane wektory cech
    stage VARCHAR(50),
    evolution_history JSONB,
    metadata_uri VARCHAR(500),
    is_tokenized BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

ğŸ”— API Endpoints

Authentication

POST /api/auth/login           # Magic link login
POST /api/auth/connect-wallet  # Link Web3 wallet
POST /api/auth/logout          # Logout user
GET  /api/auth/session         # Get current session


Users & Artists

GET    /api/users/profile      # Get user profile
PUT    /api/users/profile      # Update profile
GET    /api/artists            # List artists (with filters)
GET    /api/artists/:id        # Get artist details
POST   /api/artists            # Create artist profile
PUT    /api/artists/:id        # Update artist profile


Content & Marketplace

GET    /api/tracks             # List tracks/beats
POST   /api/tracks             # Upload new track
GET    /api/tracks/:id         # Get track details
PUT    /api/tracks/:id         # Update track
DELETE /api/tracks/:id         # Delete track

POST   /api/marketplace/list   # List item for sale
POST   /api/marketplace/buy    # Purchase item
GET    /api/marketplace/orders # Get user orders


NFT & Consciousness

POST   /api/nft/mint           # Mint consciousness NFT
GET    /api/nft/:id            # Get NFT metadata
POST   /api/consciousness      # Create/update consciousness profile
GET    /api/consciousness/:id  # Get consciousness data


AI & Recommendations

POST   /api/ai/recommend       # Get recommendations
POST   /api/ai/analyze         # Analyze consciousness compatibility
GET    /api/ai/trends          # Get trending analysis

ğŸ” Smart Contracts

DRTToken.sol (ERC-20)
solidity
contract DRTToken is ERC20, Ownable {
    uint256 public constant MAX_SUPPLY = 1_000_000_000 * 10**18;
    
    mapping(address => bool) public minters;
    
    function mint(address to, uint256 amount) external onlyMinter {
        require(totalSupply() + amount <= MAX_SUPPLY, "Max supply exceeded");
        _mint(to, amount);
    }
    
    function addMinter(address minter) external onlyOwner {
        minters[minter] = true;
    }
}


ConsciousnessNFT.sol (ERC-721)
solidity
contract ConsciousnessNFT is ERC721, Ownable {
    using Counters for Counters.Counter;
    Counters.Counter private _tokenIds;
    
    struct ConsciousnessData {
        string metadataURI;
        uint256 evolutionStage;
        bytes32 vectorHash;
        uint256 createdAt;
    }
    
    mapping(uint256 => ConsciousnessData) public consciousnessData;
    
    function mintConsciousness(
        address to,
        string memory metadataURI,
        bytes32 vectorHash
    ) external onlyOwner returns (uint256) {
        _tokenIds.increment();
        uint256 tokenId = _tokenIds.current();
        
        _mint(to, tokenId);
        
        consciousnessData[tokenId] = ConsciousnessData({
            metadataURI: metadataURI,
            evolutionStage: 1,
            vectorHash: vectorHash,
            createdAt: block.timestamp
        });
        
        return tokenId;
    }
}


Marketplace.sol
solidity
contract HHUMarketplace is ReentrancyGuard, Ownable {
    IERC20 public drtToken;
    uint256 public platformFee = 250; // 2.5%
    
    struct Listing {
        address seller;
        address nftContract;
        uint256 tokenId;
        uint256 price;
        bool active;
    }
    
    mapping(bytes32 => Listing) public listings;
    
    function createListing(
        address nftContract,
        uint256 tokenId,
        uint256 price
    ) external {
        require(price > 0, "Price must be greater than 0");
        
        IERC721 nft = IERC721(nftContract);
        require(nft.ownerOf(tokenId) == msg.sender, "Not token owner");
        require(nft.isApprovedForAll(msg.sender, address(this)), "Not approved");
        
        bytes32 listingId = keccak256(abi.encodePacked(nftContract, tokenId, block.timestamp));
        
        listings[listingId] = Listing({
            seller: msg.sender,
            nftContract: nftContract,
            tokenId: tokenId,
            price: price,
            active: true
        });
        
        emit ListingCreated(listingId, msg.sender, nftContract, tokenId, price);
    }
    
    function buyItem(bytes32 listingId) external nonReentrant {
        Listing storage listing = listings[listingId];
        require(listing.active, "Listing not active");
        
        uint256 platformCut = (listing.price * platformFee) / 10000;
        uint256 sellerAmount = listing.price - platformCut;
        
        drtToken.transferFrom(msg.sender, listing.seller, sellerAmount);
        drtToken.transferFrom(msg.sender, owner(), platformCut);
        
        IERC721(listing.nftContract).safeTransferFrom(
            listing.seller,
            msg.sender,
            listing.tokenId
        );
        
        listing.active = false;
        
        emit ItemSold(listingId, msg.sender, listing.seller, listing.price);
    }
}

ğŸ¯ User Journey Flows

1. Onboarding (Bez portfela)

1. Rejestracja email + magic link
2. UzupeÅ‚nienie profilu (alias, bio, avatar)
3. WybÃ³r typu: Artist / Fan / Investor
4. Opcjonalne: poÅ‚Ä…czenie portfela Web3
5. Claim free DRT tokens (airdrop)
6. Przewodnik po platformie


2. Onboarding (Z portfelem)

1. PoÅ‚Ä…czenie portfela (MetaMask/WalletConnect)
2. Weryfikacja adresu
3. Mint profilu NFT lub claim tokenÃ³w
4. DostÄ™p do funkcji crypto
5. Automatic consciousness profile creation


3. Marketplace Flow (Kupno)

1. Browse beats/NFTs
2. Kliknij "Buy Now"
3. WybÃ³r pÅ‚atnoÅ›ci: DRT / USD (Stripe)
4. JeÅ›li crypto: MetaMask transaction
5. JeÅ›li fiat: Stripe checkout
6. Transfer NFT + automatic royalty split
7. Email potwierdzenia + dashboard update


4. Upload & Mint Flow

1. Upload audio file
2. Add metadata (title, description, tags)
3. Choose license type
4. Set price (DRT/USD)
5. Optional: Mint as NFT
6. IPFS storage + metadata JSON
7. List on marketplace

Blockchain Event Listener
javascript
// Listen for smart contract events
const listenToMarketplaceEvents = () => {
    marketplaceContract.on('ItemSold', async (listingId, buyer, seller, price) => {
        await updateDatabase({
            listingId,
            buyer,
            seller,
            price,
            status: 'completed'
        });
        
        await sendNotifications(buyer, seller);
        await updateUserStats(buyer, seller);
    });
};


AI Recommendation Engine
javascript
// Generate recommendations based on user behavior
const generateRecommendations = async (userId) => {
    const userHistory = await getUserListeningHistory(userId);
    const consciousnessProfile = await getConsciousnessProfile(userId);
    
    const recommendations = await aiModel.predict({
        history: userHistory,
        consciousness: consciousnessProfile,
        trending: await getTrendingTracks()
    });
    
    await cacheRecommendations(userId, recommendations);
};

ğŸ“Š Analytics & KPIs

Kluczowe Metryki
javascript
const kpis = {
    // User Engagement
    MAU: 'Monthly Active Users',
    DAU: 'Daily Active Users',
    sessionDuration: 'Average session time',
    retention: {
        day1: '% users returning after 1 day',
        day7: '% users returning after 7 days',
        day30: '% users returning after 30 days'
    },
    
    // Monetization
    conversionRate: 'Paying users / Total users',
    ARPPU: 'Average Revenue Per Paying User',
    ARPU: 'Average Revenue Per User',
    GMV: 'Gross Merchandise Value',
    takeRate: 'Platform commission %',
    
    // Marketplace
    listingsPerDay: 'New listings created',
    salesConversion: 'Sales / Listings',
    averagePrice: 'Average NFT/track price',
    
    // Consciousness
    profilesCreated: 'New consciousness profiles',
    evolutionEvents: 'Consciousness evolution triggers',
    compatibilityMatches: 'Successful matchmaking'
};


Event Tracking
javascript
// Track user actions for analytics
const trackEvent = (userId, event, properties) => {
    const eventData = {
        userId,
        event,
        properties,
        timestamp: Date.now(),
        sessionId: getSessionId(),
        platform: 'web' // or 'mobile'
    };
    
    // Send to analytics pipeline
    analyticsQueue.add('track-event', eventData);
};

// Example events
trackEvent(userId, 'track_played', { trackId, duration, source: 'discovery' });
trackEvent(userId, 'nft_purchased', { tokenId, price, paymentMethod: 'DRT' });
trackEvent(userId, 'consciousness_evolved', { profileId, newStage, trigger: 'creation' });

ğŸ›¡ï¸ BezpieczeÅ„stwo

Smart Contract Security
Audyty: Minimum 1 niezaleÅ¼ny audyt przed mainnet
Reentrancy Protection: OpenZeppelin ReentrancyGuard
Access Control: Proper ownership patterns
Pausability: Emergency stop mechanism
Upgrade Patterns: Proxy contracts for critical components

Backend Security
Rate Limiting: API throttling + DDoS protection
Input Validation: Wszystkie endpoints walidowane
SQL Injection Prevention: Parameterized queries
XSS Protection: Content Security Policy
HTTPS: TLS wszÄ™dzie
Secret Management: AWS KMS + rotacja kluczy

Privacy
Data Encryption: Sensitive data encrypted at rest
Consciousness Data: End-to-end encryption
GDPR Compliance: Right to deletion, data portability
Consent Management: Explicit consent for AI features

    ports:
"6379:6379"


CI/CD Pipeline
yaml
.github/workflows/deploy.yml
name: Deploy to Production
on:
  push:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
uses: actions/checkout@v3
name: Run tests
        run: |
          npm ci
          npm run test
          npm run test:contracts
  
  deploy:
    needs: test
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
name: Deploy to Vercel
        uses: amondnet/vercel-action@v20
        with:
          vercel-token: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
          vercel-org-id: ${{ secrets.ORG_ID }}
          vercel-project-id: ${{ secrets.PROJECT_ID }}
